euery gentylman furtheraunce gentylnesse procure euer renewe noble worthynesse dayly sene eye expresse noble men endyte rede bokes olde theyr worthy myndes fede ¶ nowe late came custodye foresayd boke bryan anslay yoman seller eyght kynge henry gentyl woman excellence say whiche lyked yet made delay impresse guyse people lewde theyr prowesse dyspyse ¶ shewed foresayd boke unto lorde gentyll erle kente hym requyred theron loke counsayle put prente forthwith euer dylygente ladyes abrode sprede theyr royall fame exhorted prynte name ¶ obeyenge gladly instaunce haue done deuoyre make ende telleth howe whome cyte ladyes fyrst begon buylde capitulo primo maner haue moche vsage thynge whiche excercyse lyfe moost dy posed knowe haun tynge studye day syttynge lytell cell dyuers bokes dyuers matter aboute myne entente tyme trauayle gather consayte wayenge dyuers sentence dyuers auctours longe tyme studyed dressed vysage towarde foresayd bokes thynkynge y• tyme leue pea subtyll thynges dysporte loke vpon pleasaunt boke wrytynge poetes entente serched aboute praty boke aduenture came straunge boke handes taken kepe opened boke sawe ye intytulacyon called hym matheolus laughynge bycause sene hym often tymes herde speke hym sholde speke well reuerence woman thought maner solace wolde vysyte hym yet loked longe hym yt good moder bare called refeccyon souper wherof ye houre come purposynge se hym mornynge lefte hym yt tyme ye morowe folowynge sate agayne study dyde custome forgate put wyll effecte yt came ye nyght vysyte ye foresayd boke matheolus began rede prosede hym semed ye matter ryght pleasaunt people yt delyted euyll sayenge profyte ony edyfyenge vertue seynge wordes matter dyshonest whiche touched vysytynge came ye ende lefte hym toke hede hygher matter profyte yet syght foresayd boke howe none auctoryte engē dred newe thought whiche made grete meruayle growe courage thynkynge myght cause wherof myght come many dyuers men clerkes others haue ben ben enclyned say mouthe theyr treatyse wrytynges many slaundres blame woman theyr condycyons onely one twayne matheolus whiche amonge others hath maner reputacyon treateth maner scorne generally treaty phylosphres poetes rethorycyens whiche sholde longe reherce theyr name speketh one mouthe accordeth semble conclusyon determynynge ye condycyons woman ben fully enclyned vyces thynges thynkynge ryght depely began examyne myselfe condycyons woman naturall lyke wyse dyscuted woman who companye haunted well pryncesses grete ladyes meane gentyll woman ryght grete plentye whiche theyr grace haue tolde theyr pryuytees strayte thoughtes knowe iugement conscyence fauoure yf myght trewe many notable men one wytnesseth yet withstandynge thynges yt myght knowe longe haue sought serched coude perceyue suche iugementes myght trewe agaynst naturall condycyons ners woman argued strongly agaynst woman sayenge yt sholde grete thynge yt many famous men solempne clarkes soo hyghe grete vnderstandynge clerely seynge thynges semed sholde haue spoken wryten lyengly many place yt payne founde ony morall volume euer yt auctoure yt redde ye ende chapytres certayne clause blamynge theym onely shorte reason made conclude myne vnderstandynge symplenesse ygnoraunce ne coude knowe grete defautes semblably woman alwaye accorded truely soo reported iugement felte knowe myselfe thus thought persone halfe hymselfe came ryght grete foyson dyttyes prouerbes many dyuers auctours ye purpose yt remembred myselfe one another welle spryngynge conclusyon determyned yt god made foule thynge fourmed woman meruayllynge howe soo worshypfull werke man deyned euer make one soo abhomynable werke whiche vessell sayenge thē y• draught herbegage al euyll vyces beynge thought sprange grete dyspleasannce sorowe courage dyspraysynge myselfe womenkynde yf yt sholde shewed nature sayd suche wordes mycomplayntes ha lorde god howe may yt arre y• fayth ought doubt yt thyne infynyte wysdome veray parfyte goodnesse nothynge made yt good fourmest y• thyselfe womā ryght syngulerly y• gaue suche inclynacyons yt pleased ye yt sholde haue howe maye yt yt thou sholde haue fayled ony thynge alway se many grete occasyons thus iuged determyned cō cluded ayenst vnderstande pugnaunce yf good lorde god yt true yt womankynde haboundeth many abhomy nacyons many men wytnesseth thou sayest thyselfe yt wytnesse many forto byleue whiche ought doubte shol de true ala good lorde haddest thou made borne worlde y• mascu lyne kynde entente yt myne euclynacyons myght haue ben al haue serued better y• sholde haue arred ony thynge myght haue ben grete perfeccyon say yt men yet syth thy debonayrnesse stretche th moche towarde spare negly gence thy seruyce good lorde god dyspleased seruaunt receyueth leest rewardes lorde leest bounde seruyce suche wordes mo ynowe sayd ryght lon ge sorowfull thought god lamentacyon foly helde ryght euyll contente god made borne worlde kynde woman ¶ xp̄ine telleth howe iii ladyes appered howe yt wente reasoned fyrste comforted dyspleasure capitulo secundo sorowfull thought y• heed downe cast shamfull per sone eye full teeres holdynge myne hande vnder cheke lenynge y• pomell chayre sod • ynly sawe come downe vpon lappe stremyn ge lyght y• derke place whiche y• sone myght shyne y• houre sterte thoughe ben waked dreme dressynge heed beholde lyght fro whens myght come sawe standynge thre ladyes crowned ryght souerayne reuerence whiche shynynge theyr clere face gaue lyght vnto place meruayllynge neyther man woman consyderynge dore close vpon thyder came doubtynge leest ben fantasye haue tempted made sygne crosse forehede ful drede whiche fyrst thre laughynge began thus reason dere doughter drede ye nought come hyder nothynge contrary vnto encombred comforte haue pyte thy trouble put ygnoraunce moche blyndeth thyne vnderstādynge thou puttest fro thou knowest certayne • yence gyue faythe contrary whiche thou felest ne seest ne knowest otherwyse pluralyte straunge opynyons thou resemblest fole whiche made iape whiche slepynge ye mylle whas clothed clothynge womā make resemblaunce mocked hym wytnessed yt woman byleued theyr false saynges ye certaynte beynge howe fayre doughter thy wytte become hast thou forgoten nowe howe ye fyne golde proueth hym fornayse yt chaungeth vertue plyaunt brought dyuers facyons knowest thou yt moost meruayllous thynges moost debatous arguous yf thou wylte aduyse wyse moost hyghe thynges ben yt knowe ye celestyall thynges beholde yf grete phylosophres hath ben thou arguest agaynst thyne owne kynde haue determyned false contrary trouthe repugne one agaynst another thou thyselfe hast sene ye boke metaphisike arystotle reproueth theyr opynyons reherseth wyse plato others note agayne saynt austyne doctours ye chyrche haue done wyse arystotle partyes al called prynce phylosophres whome phylosophye naturall morall soueraynely semeth trowest al wordes phylosophres ben artycles fayth ihesu cryst maye arre poetes whiche thou spekest knowest thou well haue spoken many thynges manere fable entende moche contrary theyr sayenges sheweth maye taken rewle grammere whiche named antyphrasys whiche entendeth thus thou knowest well one sholde say syth one shrewe saye good contrary counsayle thou thy profyte theyr sayenges thou vnderstande euer theyr entente suche place blame woman peraduenture mā matheolus boke vnderstode ye many thynges taketh letter sholde pure heresye shame hym sayth onely hym others wyse ye romaunce rose whome put grete faythe bycause auctoryte maker ordre maryage whiche holy estate worshypfull ordeyned god thynge proueth clerely experyence contrary true shrewdenesse purpose syth estate grete charge blame woman euer housbande yt euer suffred suche maystrye wyfe sholde haue leue saye many vylanyes iniures put vpon woman sholde saye byleue euer thou hast sene wrytynge yu sawest neuer ye eye pure lesynges ryght shrewdely coloured thus say concludynge lefe frende folye caused ye presente opynyon nowe come agayne thyselfe take thy wytte trouble ye suche fantasyes knowe wel yt euyll saynges generally womē hurteth ye sayers ye womē ¶ xp̄ine sayth howe lady reasoned deuysed propryete wher serued tolde howe sholde buylde cyte ye helpe iij ladyes ca iij famous lady sayenge wordes ye presence whome say whiche wyttes moost vndertaken myne herynge herkenynge worthy wordes syght beholdynge grete beaute attyre reuerent porte ryght worshypfull countenaunce wyse others wyst whiche beholde soo moche thre ladyes resembled eyther payne myght knowe one sholde haue ben deceyued lesse auctoryte chere fyerse whome eyen behelde hardy sholde vndertaken grete drede semed manased euyll doer soo standynge vp syege theyr reuerence beholdynge without faynynge ony worde persone ouertaken yt coude sowne worde grete meruayle herte thynkynge myght ryght gladly yf durste wolde haue asked theyr name theyr beynge sygnyfyenge ye dyfferent septres yt eche helde theyr ryght handes whiche ryght grete rychesse wherfore come thyder yet thought worthy reason suche demaundes soo hyghe ladyes appered vnto durst manere contynued syght vpon theym halfe aferde halfe assured wordes herde saye whiche hathe cast fyrst thought yet ryght wyse lady yt reasoned whiche knewe thought spyryte hath syght thynges answered thought saynge thus dere doughter knowe ye prouydence god nothynge leueth vayne ne cometh v estable thoughe knowe celestyall thynges haunte amonge people bace worlde ye entente put ordre holde equyte stablementes made ourselfe wyll god dyuers offyces ye whiche god thre ben doughters hym borne myne offyce redresse men woman waye put agayne ryght waye come thē pryuely spyryte couertely preche teche shewynge theyr erroure whiche fayle assygne cause teche theym ye manere folowe howe sholde flee lefte yt serue showe clerely make se conscyence theyr dedes euery man woman theyr propre tatches defautes thou feest holde stede septre bryght glasse myroure bere ryght hande knowe trouthe persone loketh myroure maye knowe euery creature clerely myroure grete dygnyte without grete cause enuyronned ryche precyous stone thou seest hym beynges qualytees proporcyon measure al thynges ben know ne ne without hym may nothynge well made done yt thou desyrest knowe also offyces myne two systers yt thou seest entente wytnessynge v may certayne eche theyr owne persone shall answere theyr name theyr propryete yet cause mouynge comynge shall declared ryght make vnderstande shall done nothynge without good cause apperyn ge nothynge vayne thoughe comunely many place knowlege v cometh vnto people neuerthelesse grete loue whiche thou haste enquyre thynges veray longe contynuall studye whiche thou doest yelde thyselfe solytarye thou withdraw est worlde thou haste deserued thou deseruest vysyted comforted v thy trouble sorowe ryght dere frende thou made clerely seynge thynges defoule trouble thy courage derkenesse thought also gretter cause comynge specyal thou shalte knowe reuelacyon vnderstande entente erroure myght destroyed wolde ladyes worshypfull woman myght haue hen forthe manere place come cloystre defence agaynst wolde assayle defaute whiche foresayd ladyes famous woman haue longe tyme lefte vnclosed felde without hedge without fyndynge ony champyon theyr defence myght compare suffycyently notwithstandynge noble men ordenaunce ryght ought defende theym whiche neglygence force hathe suffred defouled ye whiche meruayl thoughe theyr enuyous enemyes outrage vylaynes assaylled dyuers craftes haue ye vyctory agaynst theyr warre defaute defence yt cyte stronge yt myght sone taken yf founde resystence ¶ vniuste cause myght goten cōtynuaunce hym yt pledeth wtout party ryght symple debonayre ladyes ye ensample pacyence whiche god cōmaūdeth hath suffred frendely grete iniuryes yt moche ye mouthe many theyr hādes wrytynge haue suffred moche wronge thus reporte god theyr good ryght yet nowe tyme theyr iuste cause put ye handes pharao therfore bytwene v thre ladyes yt thou seest moued pyte come tell certayne buyldynge made manere cloystre cyte strongely wrought mason handes well buylded whiche predestynate make stable helpe counsayle whiche shall none enhabyte onely ladyes good fame woman worthy praysynges vertue shall founde walles cyte shall strongely shytte ¶ xp̄ine telleth howe lady deuyfed cyte commytted make yt stabled helpe begyn walles cloystre aboute tolde name capitulo iiij thus fayre doughter yt prerogatyue gyuen amonge al woman make fortefye cyte ladyes whiche thou shalte take vpon make foundement parfytely conclude hym thou shal te receyue v thre wyne water clere welle shall delyuer mater ynoughe stronger durable ony marbre cyment shal better thā thou shalte haue shall thy cyte ryght fay without pere perpetuall durynge worlde ¶ haste yu redde yt kynge troy founded grete cyte troye ye helpe appolo mynerue neptune whiche people tyme trowed theym goddes also howe cadmus founded cyte thebe ye mynestracyon goddes al cy tee space tyme ouerthrowne ben tourned ruyne prophecye verray sybylle neuer cyte whiche thou shalte founde shall brought nought ne shall fall alway endure prosperyte maulgre enuyous enemyes thoughe fou ght withall many dyuers assaultes shal neuer taken ne ouercome ¶ somtyme ye royalme amosonye begonne ye ordynaun ce entrepryse dyuers woman grete courage whiche despysed bondage hystoryes bereth wytnesse longe tyme mayntayned vnder sygnyouryes dyuers quenes ryght noble ladyes ye whiche chose selfe gouerned ryght fayre well gre te strengthe maynteyned lordshyp neuer thelesse thoughe grete myght puyssaunce tyme theyr domynacyon conquered grete parte oryent landes nyghe put drede wyse countre grece doubted whiche tyme y• foure countrees y• worlde yt within processe tyme puyssaunce royalme manere worldely lordshyppes den tyme nowe onely ye cyte shal moche stronger buyldyn ge thou hast make ye whiche begyn commytted ye delyberacyon amonge v thre ladyes togyder delyuer morter durable without corrupcyon make stron foundementes grete walles aboute lyfte vp hyghe large grete towres stronge castelles dyked bastyled barred moche perteyneth cyte grete defen ce deuyse thou shalte set grete dep nesse endure longer thou shalte lyfte vp walles hyghe yt worlde shal drede doughter thus haue nowe tolde ye cause comynge ye entente yt thou take credence sayenge nowe wyll yt thou lerne name sowne yt whi che onely thou shalte knowe yt thou hast y• wylte folowe myne ordynaūces mynystresse thy nede ytyu myght yestereuen na med dame reason nowe aduyse ye yf yu good conduyte say ye tyme ¶ xp̄ine telleth howe seconde lady tolde name wherof serued howe sholde helpe make masonry cyte ladyes ca v whan lady aboue sayd accheued worde laysoure answere seconde lady began answere manere called ryghtwysnesse whiche hathe dwellynge heuen erthe sone beme lyghtnynge shynynge god messangere goodnesse haunte amonge iuste persones counsayle thynge well yelde euery man say sustayne trouthe ryght poore people innocentes greue others vsurpacyon sustayne renowne ben accused without cause shelde defence seruauntes god call punycyon euyll folkes make gyue alowe trauayllers rewarde good doer god maketh open secretes frendes theyr aduocate heuen shynynge lyne yt thou seest holde stede septre ryght hande y• ryght rewle y• departeth ryght wronge sheweth dyfference bytwene good euyll foloweth shall goo waye staffe pea reconsyleth good vpon lene smyteth beteth euyl doer sholde saye lyne thynges lymytted dygnytees hym ben infynyte soo vnderstande shall serue wel thou shalte haue nede hym measure buyldynge cyte commytted make sayd cyte make stone werke make within hyghe towres hyghe pa layces compace housynge mansyons stretes place thynges couenables helpe put suffycyent people within foresayd cyte thus come thyne helpe syster reason noble lady whiche thou seest boholde myne offyce nowe dysmaye thou grete largenesse longe cyrcuyte closynge walle helpe god v thou shalte buylde people ryght well fayre without leuynge ony voyde thynge wt fayre mansyons stronge herbegages ¶ xp̄ine telleth howe thyrde lady tolde wherfore serued howe wolde helpe make hyghe bataylmentes towres cyte people noble ladyes ca vi spake thyrde lady whiche sayd ryght thus xp̄ine ryght dere frende iustyce synguler doughter god beynge procedeth purely propre persone dwellynge heuen erthe helle heuen glorye sayntes blessyd soules erthe departe gyue euery man porcyon good euyll hathe deserued helle punycyon euyl people bowe parte frende fere grete wyl pyte prayer thretnynge cruelte moueth myne offyce onely iuge departe make y• payment euery mannes ryghtfull deseruynge susteyne thynges estate without may thynge stablysshed god god one selfe thynge foloweth maye fayle waye sure teche euery man womā holsome vnderstandynge yf byleue teche hym chastyce knowe reproue hymselfe fyrst another yt wolde sholde done hym departe thynges without fauoure saye trouthe fle hate lesynges put away vycyous thynges vessell fyne golde yt thou seest ryght hande made ye guyse rounde measure god fader gaue serueth measure euery man lyueray suche meryte ought haue marked ye floure deluce trynyte yelded hym iuste porcyons maye noo man complayne measure men worlde haue measure whiche saye dependeth come th myne falsely measure often tymes vnder shadowe theyr measure alwaye iuste large ▪ lytel others myght holde longe tale ynoughe propryetees myne offyce shortly say especyall amonge vertues al referre amonge v iij ladyes thou seest one selfe thynge may none v without fyrst dysposeth seconde ordeyneth putteth werke thyrde perfourmeth bryngeth ende thus stabled helpe wyll v thre perfytely make thy cyte myne offyce shall make ye hyghe roffes thy towres mansyons herbegages whiche shall fyne golde shynynge bryght shall people ryght worthy ladyes shal suche shall haue prerogatyue honoure amonge woman ye moost excellence shall yelde thyne owne helpe parfyte fortefyenge closynge stronge gate whiche shall go seke heuen shall delyuer vnto keyes myne owne handes ¶ xp̄ine telleth howe spake iij ladyes ca vij wordes abouesayd ended whiche herkened grete entente iij ladyes whiche drawne fro entyerly dyspleasaunce theyr comynge sodaynly fell downe theyr feete onely knee flatte theyr grete excellence kyssynge y• erthe aboute theyr feete worshyppynge theym goddess began myneoryson praysynge wyse lady souerayne dygnyte lanternesse heuen gyuynge ly ght erthe welles paradyse ioy ben blessyd wherof come hyghnesse suche humylyte ye haue vouched saufe come frome hyghe syeges shynynge trones troubled tabernacle dar ke symple ygnoraunt studye whiche maye yelde couenable thankynges suche benefyce whiche haue rayne dewe swete wordes fallen vpon departed tempered drynesse myne vnderstandynge y• feleth hym nowe redy burgyn put newe plantes dysposed bere fruyte profytable vertue delectable smellynge howe shal done suche grace shall receyue gyfte worde make fortefye nowe ryght worlde suche newe cyte saynt thomas appostle made deuyne grace heuen ryche palays y• kynge ynde feble wytte ne knoweth crafte ne measure ne studye pratyke buyldynge yf thynges possybylyte connynge nowe myne vnderstādynge sholde taken suffycyent strengthe f • ble woman body put grete thynge werke yet neuertheles ryght redoubted ladyes howe yt meruayllynge newe tydynges straunge knowe well y• nothynge impossyble god ought doubte thynges y• euer taken hande counsayle helpe thre wel fayre ended thus worshyp ped god al power ladyes moche haue worshypped sta bled noble commyssyon y• whiche receyue grete gladnesse se chamberere redy obey nowe cōmaunde pleasure ¶ xp̄ine telleth howe commaundement dame reason began dygge erthe make foundement ca viij reason y• noble lady answered sayd nowe ryse doughter without abydynge go felde scryptures shall loū ded cyte ladyes playne countre fruytefull fruytes swete water ben founde grounde haboundeth good thynges take py coys thyne vnderstandynge dygge strong ly make grete dyke aboute thou seest y• trace lyne shall helpe bere y• erthe vpon myne owne sholders obeye theyr commaūdemente dressed lyghtly felynge selfe y• vertue stronge lyght wente came foresayd felde began dyke dygge af ter sygne picoys inquisycyon fyrst worke done wyse ¶ madame lesse wyse howe dyde y• perteynynge wyl take hede semeth one myght se noble ladyes theyr wydo whode haue susteyned suffycyently well kepte iurysdyc • yon ryght theyr lordeshyppes theyr housbandes dyde tyme lyuynge well loued theyr subiectes better doubte dyspleasaunce men y• ben many woman y• haue better vnderstandynge men haue whiche yf theyr housbandes byleued suche vnderstandynge myght haue tourned theym grete profyte yet thoughe woman communely medle dede iugement ne pronounce cause partyes theym force moche haue lesse charge theyr soules theyr bodyes howe thynge necessary punysshe y• euyll doer ryght vnto euery man ben men ynowe suche offycers myght wy y• neuer knowne theyr moders yf go ryght waye god knoweth whiche ony fraude theyr punycyon lytell ¶ altercacyons argumentes xp̄ine dame reason ca xiiij certes madame ye say ryght wel reason ben ryght well sow • yn ge courage yet thoughe theyr vnderstandynge proued woman haue feble bodyes tendre myghty dedes strengthe nature ben cowardes one thynge maketh moche lesse degree auctoryte kynde woman iugement men wyll saye moche body imperfyte euery thynge moche abredged made lesse vertue thou folowest y• lesse prayse ¶ answere dere doughter thys folowynge good susteyned without fayle one seeth often tymes y• nature hathe restrayned ony thynge frome body y• hathe fourmed rewardeth yt body thynge moche valoure thus womā imparfyte shap beaute im potencye feblenes membres sygne y• recompenseth thynge worth yt hath berafte ensample sayd grete phylosophre arystotle whiche ryght lewde shap one eye hygher straunge vysage yet thoughe ony deformyte body shap true ly nature recompensed hym ryght gretely vnderstandynge retentyfe felynge appereth antentyke wrytynges yt recompensynge grete wytte valoure thā thoughe body lyke vnto absolon wyse one maye say grete emperoure alexandre yt lytell body yet gre te vertue courage appered many others promyse fayre loue yt grete stronge body causeth vertuous myghty courage cometh vertuous strē gethe maners yt gyuen god whiche graun teth nature leue creature reasonables thā others gyfte hyd vnderstandynge courage onely strengthe body membres thus knowe often tymes y• grete men ynowe stronge membres se latch faylyn ge recrayed others haue ben lytell fe ble body y• ben hardy full stronge wyse vertues y• hardynes suche strengthe god nature hathe done ynoughe woman y• hath gyuen im potencye y• leest ben agreably excused yt defaute moche yt horry ble crueltees y• wronges grete greues extorcyons whiche done y• worlde bycau se strength shal haue suche punyssh mentes suche case requyreth sholde haue ben ryght good y• soules man y• myght haue passed pylgrymage worlde feble body woman truely saye come agayne purpose y• yf nature gyuen grete strengthe membres woman body y• recompenseth ryght well y• gyuen vertuous inclynacyon yt loue god dredefull naturally cō trary commaundementes otherwyse dothe kynde alwayes aduyse dere doughter howe semeth y• god lyst showe degree men thoughe y• say y• moche womē haue grete stren gthe hardynesse corporall communely men haue y• ought byleue y• al bodely strengthe hardynesse shytte fro kynde womā appereth many woman shewed grete courage strengthe hardynesse vndertake maner stronge thynges accheue lyke dyde grete men solem • ne conquerours whō made grete mencyon wrytynges shall remembre y• ensample fayre doughter nowe haue ordeyned arayed y• pytte grete large haue borne vpō sholdres ryght grete burden rubrysshe erthe tyme yt thou sette grete stronge stone foundement y• walles cyte ladyes nowe take thy truell thy plumbe wt thy lyne make y• redy werke strong ly y• masonry grete dylygence se gre te large stone whiche wyll y• y• fyrste set foundement thy cyte knowe yt na ture herselfe hathe pourtrayed sygnes astrologye alowed werke nowe drawe lytell abacke shall cast hym ¶ quene semyramys ca xv semyramys woman ryght grete vertue dede grete vycto ryous courage vndertakynge entrepryses hauntynge de de armes whiche excellent people whiche pay nymes sayd grete myght strengthe hadde bothe vpon lande vpon see syster vnto grete god iupyter doughter auncyent god saturnus whiche called god lande see lady wyfe man vygure strengthe surmounted lady habounded ryght hardy cou rage ne doubted payne ne aferde perylles put herselfe thynges suche excellence y• ouercame aduersaryes y• trowed put wydowhode cōquestes y• whiche dredde doubted armes yt kepte onely y• countres conquered wt ryght grete armye wente vpon y• lande ethyope whiche ouercame grete strengthe put vnder subieccyon ioyned empyre then wen te stron ger dyuers defense lete make aboute lar ge depe dyke semyramys tyme chambre maydens aboute k • mynge heed happened tydynges came y• one royalmes began rebell agaynst lyfted vp herselfe sware puyssaunce tresse heed sholde neuer tressed whiche vntressed tyll tyme venged iniury put agayne londe subieccyon made • ne men arme grete multytude wente vpon rebelles meruaylous strengthe put vnder subieccyon thus subiectes dradde neuer syth durste moue fote rebell whiche noble dede couragyous longe tyme gaue wytnesse grete ymage made brasse gylte rychely lyfte vp vpon hyghe pyller ba bylone whiche represented pryncesse holdynge swerde hande one sydes heed tressed y• quene foūded edyfyed newe dyuers cytees stronge place accō plysshed many grete dedes moche yt neuer wryten man grete courage ne meruaylous werkes worthy mynde trouthe many blameth ought ryght yf ben lawe yt toke owne sone housbande yt goten nynus lorde cause moued ij pryncypally one wolde haue empyre none lady crowned saue onely herselfe y• whiche sholde haue ben sone wedded ony lady cause semed mā worthy haue wyfe saue onely ow ne sone yet cause y• gretter thrughe whi somwhat excused y• lawe y• people lyued y• lawe nature one durste doo another without mysse takynge whiche herte perceyued desyred doubte thou ght ben euyll ony blame sholde fall therof grete soo hyghe courage loued moche worshyp wolde neuer haue done nowe fyrst stone set foundement cyte nowe con uenyent hen forthe set sewyngly stone quantyte auaunce buyldynge ¶ amozones capitulo xvi lande towarde ende europe grete see holde th worlde whiche lande called syche sychye happened somtyme y• countre force warre despoyled y• yonge men dwel lynge countree woman place sawe lost theyr housbandes theyr bretherne theyr kynnesmen none lefte olde men chyldren assembled grete courage toke counsayle bytwene aduysed conclusyon tyme forth wolde maynteyne theyr lordshyppes without ony subieccyon mē made suche commaundement maner man sholde entre theyr iurysdyc • yon▪ yet haue lygnage sholde go y• nerte countre certayne season yere sholde tourne home agayne theyr coun tre yf delyuered ony sone sholde sende vnto theyr faders yf mayde chyldren wolde nourysshe themselfe perfourme theyr ordynaunce chose ij moost noble ladyes amonge crowned quenes whiche one called lampheto marpasye ne chased theyr countre y• mankynde lefte bothe yonge olde yt armed grete batayle ladyes maydens wente vpon theyr enemyes wasted theyr lande fyre armrs none myght resyst speke shortely auenged dethe theyr frendes full notably way began woman syche sychye bere armes y• whiche syth called amozonnes moche say vnpapped suche manere y• noble woman lytell maydens theyr lyfte pappes cutte certayne crafte y• sholde combred bere shelde gentylwomē theyr ryght pappes cut away shote easely wente moche delytynge crafte armes encrea sed forte ryght moche theyr countre theyr royalmes moche theyr fame wente aboute haue touched ye wente dyuers countrees eche theym ledynge grete hoost dyde moche y• conquered grete parte europe countre ayfe put vnder subieccyon many dyuers countres ioyned theyr lordshyppes founded many cytees townes lyke wyse ayse cyte ephese whiche longe tyme hathe ben grete renowne two quenes marpasye dyed fyrst batayle thē amozones crowned doughter place noble mayde fayre whiche named synoppe whiche grete courage hyghe y• y• dayes lyfe dysdeyned cou pled man remayned styll maybe al lyfe none loue charge onely excersyse armes y• grete pleasunce myght satysfyed assayle conquere landes royalmes moder gretly venged moche countre slayne put swerde wasted lande conquered ¶ ye quene amozonye thamaris ca xvii thus thou mayste howe amozones began maynteyned longe tyme theyr lordshyppes ryght worshypfully whiche made quenes successyon one another yf ryght worshypful ladyes whiche name rowe myght tourne reders grete noyaunce shall suffyse speke y• pryn cypalles whiche one called thama rye ryght hardy wyse sage who wytte cautele strengthe cyrrus stronge mygh ty kynge perse ouercome taken whi che conquered grete babylone wyse grete parte y• worlde wolde many conquestes done goo vpon lande amozones hope haue put vnder subieccyon wherof happened wyse y• quene knewe spy e kynge cyrrus wolde come vpō grete strengthe people ought suffycyently conquere worlde aduysed sholde impossyble dyscomfyte theyr hoost strengthe armes con uenyent laboure cautele wente worshypfull capytayne knewe y• cyrrus entred londe y• whiche suffred lete hym passe londe without ony gayne saynge made arme damoyselles ryght good ordynaū ce put dyuers busshmentes vpon y• moun tayues y• woodes cyrrus myght passe none way abode tha mary ryght stylly hoostes vnto y• ty cyrrus people come y• strayte wayes forestes amonge y• craggy roches thrughe must nedes passe lady sawe tyme made hastely blowe trompette cyrrus ryght sore abasshed whiche toke hede hymselfe sodeynly sawe hym assayled euery parte ladyes vpon moun taynes threwe downe grete roches vpon whiche myght go nother forwarde ne backe war de dyuersyte countre y• busshmentes whiche slewe y• people downe ryght feruently y• wolde haue yssued strayte passage myght gather togyder busshment y• behynde smyten sondre stronge roches dethe people cyrrus taken commaundement quene lefte alyue baron hym made come pauylyon y• dyscomfyture grete wrathe hym one maydens slayne y• way wolde haue mercy cyrrus baron made smyte theyr hedes hym sayd hym cyrrus whiche thy crueltees neuer satys fyed y• blode man nowe thou mayst drynke thy wyll made sinyte heed cast basyne whiche made gather blode lordes fayre dou ghter dere frende thynges brynge remembraunce affermeth matter y• haue tolde notwithstandynge thou knowest well thyselfe hast rehersed another tyme thy boke y• mutacyon fortune y• wyse thyne epystle othea shall say yet folowynge ¶ howe stronge hercules theseus wente vpon amozones howe ij ladyes nal • pe ypolyte almoost ouercome capitulo xviij sholde say ye strengthe theyr bodyes prowe • se armes ladyes amozonye whiche countrees dredde doubted anone y• londe gre ce whiche farre then y• tydynges wen • e howe ladyes seased destroy landes wasted countres yf wolde yelde theym ryght soone vnto theym howe withstande theyr enemyes grece aferde doubtynge landes theym sholde stretche shorte tnme vnto theyr countre grece floure hercules meruayllous stronge man whi che tyme dyde meruaylles strength euer man dyde borne woman whome made mencyon hystoryes fought gyauntes lyon serpentes monstres ryght mer • ayllous vyctory saye shortely stronge y• neuer man lyke hym strength excepte sampson le forte hercules sayd y• good abyde tyl ladyes amo • onye came vpon moche better go vpon fyrst y• lete ordeyne grete nauye shyppes assembled a▪ grete com pany yonge lusty men go thyder grete haste theseus worshypfull wyse man whiche kynge athene knewe tydynges sayd sholde go without hym assembled grete hoost hoost hercules assem bled put see towarde coun tre amozonye approched countre hercules notwithstandynge meruay lous strengthe hardynesse grete host people durste take porte day ne co downe vpon lande moche strengthe amozones blowen aboute dyuers countrees meruayle say byleue yf soo many hystoryes brynge wytnesse yt hathe ben many wor shypfull men ouercome woman hercules hoost abode tyll darke nyght co houre come eue ry mortall creature ought take rest slepe hoost lepte lande entred countre began sette fyre cytees townes slewe woman yt toke hede theyr comynge meane tyme grete y• crye amonge y• people slowe renne theyr harnoys al maner woman moost hardyest renne amonge y• people towarde y• see syde vpon theyr enemyes ¶ reygned vpon amozones quene orthya y• whiche lady ryght grete worthynesse conquered many landes moder y• worshypfull quene pantasylya shall made mencyon quene orthya crowned ye cheualrous quene anthyoppe y• whiche maynteyned y• amozones grete dy • yplyne armes cheualrye passynge wyse hardye tyme soo quene orthya herde tydynges howe grekes come nyght fyghtynge lande alway sleynge people deme yt wrothe thought auenged vpon theyr male talent anone manasynge dredde commaunded make redy batayle one myght se ladyes busy renne theyr har noys assembled aboute theyr quene tyme clere daye come quene armed herselfe abode put ordre bataylles hostes ij worshypful maydens souerayne strength cheualrye hardynesse wyse aboue many others whiche y• one called manalyppe ipolyte ryght nyghe kynne quene abode onely co mynge theyr quene fast myght armed theyr speres theyr handes theyr shel de stronge elemphant hangynge vpon theyr neckes mounted vpon theyr well rennynge cour sers wente ryght fast rennynge towarde y• porte grete hete y• supprysed wt wrathe berynge lowe theyr speres bare thrughe y• best y• grekes knowe manalyppe towarde hercules ipolyte thesens whether wrathe apered wel notwithstandynge y• grete strengthe hardynesse grete courage strongly maydens hurte grete encountre eche theym bete theyr knyght also fell yt syde soone myght recouered selfe ranne vpon good swerdes worshyp ought ladyes haue y• suche ij woman beten ij ye best knyghtes yt ye worlde thynge sholde credyble trewe y• many antentyke doc tour bereth wytnesse doctours meruayllynge themselfe aduenture excusynge specyally hercules cōsyderynge outragyous strengthe sayth yt beholdynge hors yt lepte ye grete hurte y• stroke trowed yf ben • ote sholde haue ben throwne downe ij knyghtes ashamed thus betē ij maydens notwtstandynge maydens fought wt theyr swerdes ayenst ij knyghtes strōgly y• batayle endured longe ▪ yet y• last • uayle yt maydens takē ought lyke stroke bytwene thē pryse thought gretely honoured hercules thesens gladder thā takē cyte helde theyr shyppes refresshe vnarme thought well employed theyr wyll sawe vnarmed fayre semely doubled theyr ioye toke neuer pray y• agreable kepte grete ioy plea saunce came quene vpon grekes wt grete hoost y• tydynges came two maydens taken mer uayllously sorowful yet doubte shol de harme ladyes taken yf wente vpon rested sente ij baronnesses badde put theyr fynaunce ij ladyes mo che pleased wolde sende vnto hercules theseus receyued messageres grete worshyp answered theym courtoysly yf quene wolde make small pea bothe baronnesses sholde promyse sholde neuer arme agaynst grekes theyr good frendes grekes wolde promyse wyse wolde yelde home ij ladyes quyte without hauynge ony raunsome saue theyr harnoys onely wolde ha ue worshyp remembraūce euer vyctory vpon ladyes y• quene desyre haue ij damoyselles agayne loued mo che constrayned make pea y• grekes soo matter entreated accorded bytwene y• quene came vnarmed ryght fayre company ladyes maydens ryche araye sawe neuer suche grekes mette fee sted made sure pea bytwene moche ioy made yet noyed gretely thesens delyuer ipolyte smyten grete loue soo hercules prayed requyred quene moche hym graunted thesens take ipolyte vnto wyfe sholde lede countre weddynges made worshypful ly grekes departed thesens ledde home ypolyte whiche sone warde called ipolytus whiche knyght grete worshyp chosen mā amon ge many knowne grece pea made neuer gretter ioye neuer noo thynge doubted ¶ quene pantassylea howe wente socours troye ca xix longe tyme lyued noble quene orthya grete prosperyte hel de lande amozonye moche encreased theyr puyssaunce ryght olde dyed crowned noble doughter ryght worshypfull pantassylle whiche aboue others bare crowne wytte pryce wysdome worthynesse lady ne uer wery bere armes ne fyght theyr lordshyp encreased euer tested neuer tyme moche dredde enemyes durst none abyde lady hyghe courage dysdeyned neuer coupled mā mayde lyfe ¶ tyme grete warre grekes agaynst troyans grete fame floured thrughe y• worl de ryght grete worshyp knyghthode ector troy moost manly worl de moost excellent al grace vsage gladly euery frende wolde desyre vysyte lyke pantassylle whiche thyefe ladyes y• worlde whiche herde saye contynuelly grete goodnesse worshypful ector loued hym worshypfully ryght grete loue aboue thynges desyred se hym fulfyll desyre departed royalme grete haste ryght noble company ladyes damoyselles grete prowesse ryght rychely armed toke way towarde troy whiche lytell ryght ferre yet thought longe trauaylable herte y• loueth wel ca y• porte troy aryued noble pā tassylle yet late foūde ec tor deed whiche slayne achylles lyenge wayte hym y• batayle perysshed y• floure knyghthode troy que ne pātassylle receyued grete worshyp kynge pryamus quene eccuba wyfe theyr lordes yet herte alway y• sawe neuer ector lyue whiche caused yt myght nothynge reioy ce yet ye kynge ye quene whiche without seasynge sorowed y• dethe theyr sone ector sayd yt syth myght shewe hym lyue yt wolde showe hym deed ledde y• temple made sepulture y• noble ryche y• euer ony hystory made mency made chapell ryght ryche golde precyous stone hyghe awter theyr goddes sate ye body ector chayre whiche bawmed couered y• semed vysybly y• lyue holdynge swerde hande semynge al way yt fyers vysage manased grekes clo thed garment grete large tyssue embrowdred precyous stone traylynge y• erthe couered y• partyes bynethe whiche plunged fyne bawme whiche yelded meruayllous swetnes ye troyans helde body grete worshyp ben one theyr goddes wt lyght ware clerely brēnynge ry chesse wtout nombre thyder led quene pantassylle whiche sone y• chapel opened sawe body ector kneled dow ne saluynge hym ben lyue wente nere beholdynge y• vysage begā saye suche wordes wepynge ¶ ha floure excellence knyghthode worlde grounde y• endynge worthynesse maye hense forthe auaunte hym ony prowesse stretche • werde syth y• nowe quenche • lyght ensample soo grete hyghnesse ala houre borne arme cursed durst outragyous cou rage despoyle worlde grete treasoure ¶ ryght noble prynce wherfore fortune contrary ben nyghe whē false traytoure slewe made suche wayte vpon persone ben wolde haue wayted vpon persone myselfe yet ye lyue wolde byleue dethe sholde reuenged ¶ ha grete wrathe sorowe myne herte feleth se thus without puyssaunce speke desy red moche se nowe syth maye none wyse swere al hyghe goddes byleue promyse well afferme dere lorde y• whyle lyfe shall endure youre dethe shall venged vpon grekes thus knelynge y• body pantassylle spake hyghe y• grete company lordes ladyes che • alrye myght wepte pyte coude full euyll departe then yet last kyssynge han de whiche helde swerde departed saynge ¶ worthynesse knyghthode whiche semed well ydur lyfe y• representacyon body bereth wytnesse grete excel lence anone departed wepynge ryght tenderly soone myght armed lepte y• cyte wt hoost ryght nobly arayed agaynst grekes y• syege saye shortely y• dyde without fayle yf lyued longe wolde haue done ny meruaylles armes wolde tour ne homewarde wolde fyght pyrrus y• y• sone achylles ryght manly kny ght hāde moche bete hȳ woūded hym y• almost slayne grete pay ne rescowed people deed man borne y• felde grekes trowed neuer sholde escape wherfore made moche sorowe yf hadde hate fader shewed well y• sone neuerthelesse ke shorte tale done moche armes dyuers iourneys people y• grekes vndernethe pyrrus y• amended woundes meruayllous shame sorowe thus beten soo foule womā ordeyned people hoost whiche ryght grete prowesse sholde attende none thynge y• batayle saue onely enclose pantassyllee bytwene put people wolde slayne owne hande promysed yf myght thus gyue grete gyftes thynge accomplysshe y• people pyrrus put grete payne longe tyme myght happen • dred soo moche come nyghe y• grete stroke gaue yet come conclusyon applyed y• toke hede thynge sawe iournay dyde meruayllous dedes armes myght nere hande suffyse ector yf ben lyue reason ought wery enclosed amonge departed batayle sore oppressed ladyes myght socoure notwithstandynge ryght meruayllous vertue strengthe wolde haue defended brake harnoys smote quarter helme pyrrus sawe y• heed bare whiche yelowe heere appered gaue grete stroke y• clefte sondre y• heed brayne thus ended worshypfull pantassylle grete losse troyans grete sorowe countre whiche made grete sorowe lamentacyon neuer syth reygned none suche vpon amozones thenne bare bodye home owne countre ¶ thus thou mayst began royalme woman maynteyned grete puyssaūce whiche endured y• space viij hondred yeres thou thyselfe mayst note se rede hystoryes nom bre whiche may renne syth theyr begynnynge tyll conquest grete alexandre y• conquered al y• worlde whiche tyme appered y• en dured y• reygne lordshyp y• amozones y• hystory hym maketh mencyon howe wente royalme howe receyued quene • ladyes alexādre longe tyme destruccyon troye y• wyse iiij hondred yeres foundacyon rome whiche longe tyme af ter y• sayd destruccyon troy wherfore yf thou wylte take leysoure brynge togyder hy storyes calcule tymes nombre thou shalte fynde royalme lorde shyp woman endured ryght longe space thou mayst note al lordshyppes y• hath ben worlde whiche space moche tyme hath endured one shall fynde nota ble prynces quantyte ne hath ne natable dedes done y• quenes ladyes realme ¶ cenobye quene palmurenes ca xx worshypfull woman onely amozones y• valyaūt cenobye ought lesse fame worthynes y• quene palmurenes lady noble bloode yssued ptholomees kynges egypte lady apperynge youthe grete cou rage knyghtly inclynacyon soone strengthed myght man kepe wolde leue dwellyn ge townes closyd palayces royall chambres enhabyte woodes forestes whiche place swerde gurde abou te dartes grete dylygence tosle wylde beestes hertes hyndes began fyght lyon beres many wylde beestes assayled without drede ouercame meruayllously lady helde payne lye woodes ubtynge nothynge vpon harde erthe hote colde ne greued trace y• strayte passage y• forestes graue vpon y• moū taynes dyke valays rennynge y• bestes lady dyspraysed carnall loue longe tyme refused maryage yt wolde kepe vyrgynyte yet y• last constrayned kynne toke housbande kynge palmurenes grete beaute soueraynly body vysa ge noble cenobye whiche set lytell beaute fortune fauourable inclynacyon yt consented haue housbande corespondent ynoughe condyons kynge whiche knyghtly man hadde grete luste conquere strengthe armes oryent ye empyres aboute hym tyme ualeryan auguste labour y• exercyse knyghthode kynge named ordonet stabled herode sone another woman conduyte one par te hoost takynge hede agaynst sayd sa pore kynge perce whiche tyme occupyed mesopotame ordeyned yt parte sholde go vpon hym cenobye wyfe wt another grete parte hoost hymselfe sholde go parte thyrde par te hoost soo departed suche ordynaunce shall saye ende matter suche thou mayst se y• hystoryes lady cenobye myghtely suche hardynesse vertue gate dyuers bataylles agaynst kynge vyctorye prowesse put mesopotame vnder subieccyon housbande besyeged sopore kynge perce owne cyte toke hym strengthe concubynes cō quered grete haboundaunce rychesse ¶ vyctorye happened yt housbande slayne one owne kynnes men enuye reygned vpon hym yet lady noble courage toke possessyon empyre chyldren whiche yet yonge put selfe see royall empresse toke therof gouernannct grete vertue charge say gouerned grete wytte dyscyplyne knyghthode galeryan clau dyan emperoures rome thought oc cupyed parte oryent ye romaynes dur ste neuer vndertake ony thynge agaynst wyse egypcyans ne y• arabyens ne armony doubted puyssaunce grete fyer • enesse helde theym contente kepe medle ferther lady worshypped prynces people obeyed loued knyghtes dred doubted whē rode people ofte tymes happened wolde neuer speke hoost harnoys backe helme heed batayle made armure ledde charyot notwithstandynge kynges vsed guyse alway rode vpon well rennynge courser often tymes wolde ryde vnknowne espye enemyes folke noble lady cenobye yt passed knyghtes worlde yt tyme dyscyplyne crafte knyghthode ¶ also passed ladyes noblesse good condycyons honest lyfe ryght sobre soueraynely demeanynge yet notwithstandynge made often tymes grete feestes vn baron straungers magnyfycence holden royall largesse thynges grete gyftes fayre coude well drawe people loue benyuolence alway souerayne chastyte kepte onely men wyse wolde lye housbande hauynge yssue shewed openly wolde lye hym yt felte chylde entente appered outwarde sholde afferme yt inwarde wolde neuer ony vycyous man sholde haunte courte wolde yt al wolde desyre stande good grace vertuous well condycyoned dyde grete honoure people theyr worthy nesse vertues myne armes ye shall folowe haue ordeyned conestable ye shal baron answered bad com maunde ryght good herte wolde laboure lete make well ordeyned hoost syth put wel hor sed sone bytwene armes baron al hoost enemyes perceyued began saye one ano ther se grete meruayle yesternyght appered woode forest nyghe v se nowe ryght grete thycke woode ye others yt behelde thynge sayd must nedes yt woode ben longe tyme myght none otherwyse haue ben beestyss haue perceyued se woode belle hors pastured myght haue made certayne deuysed thought ne uer trechery sodeynly quenes hoost cast away theyr braunches yt semed theyr enemyes wode appered knyghtes ar med ranne vpon done sodaynly yt theyr enemyes leysoure arme theyr beddes wente theyr lodgynges slewe toke theym coude fynde thus vyctory wytte good quene fredegonde ¶ mayde camylle ca xxiij woman worshyp knyght hode myght tell ynoughe noble mayde camylle noo lesse worthy sayd camylle doughter ryght auncyent kynge uoulques named machabyus borne moder dyed anone fader dysheryted owne people rebelled agaynst hym soo moche troubled hym constrayned fle sauynge lyfe soo bare nothynge wt hym saue onely yonge doughter loof grete loue came passe ouer grete ryuere myght chose must nedes passe grete myschyefe coude fynde counsayle helpe lytel doughter passe whē thought ynoughe toke grete ryndes tree made vessell lytell bote put lytell doughter within bounde ye vessell good rope arme put ryuere swymmynge trayled easely vessell hym doughter passed ouer water woodes lyued longe durste go none waye drede enemyes nourysshed doughter mylke wylde bestes vnto tyme well strengthed skynnes ye beestes slewe couered bothe hym doughter none bedde ne couerynge skynnes bestes whē waxed moche began warre wylde stes sle slynges stone wolde renne truely se well yt true god worshypped hath gyuen vnderstandynge woman comprehensyfe thynges vnderstande knowe holde yet yt one seeth people ynowe yt haue ryght subtyll wytte redy fele vnderstande yt one wolde showe ben subtyl felynge retentyfe yt scyence yt open ynoughe whiche hauntynge scole geteth ryght grete clargye neuerthelesse ben many also yt grete reputacyon amōge clarkes full scyence yt haue lytell wysdome maners worldely gouernaunce wherof haue grete meruayle doubte introduccyon scyence techeth y• good cōdycyons vertues wolde knowe ryght fayne lady yf pleased vnderstandynge womā whiche ynoughe semeth proues se takynge retentyfe subtyll thynges scyences others ben wolde wyte yf theyr vnderstandynge prompte abyle thynges yt prudence techeth y• knowe haue aduyse vpon yt whiche best yt ought leest remē braunce thynges passed y• whiche one maye y• experte yt ensample yt one haue wyse syght gouernaunce present thynges one haue pourueyaunce vpon thynges come thynges semeth techeth prudence ¶ answere thou sayst trewe doughter prudence whiche thou spekest knowe yt cometh nature man womā lesse allyke howe dothe moche yt naturally ben prudent thou mayst knowe yt two strengthes togyder ben resystynge thā euery strengthe hymselfe therfore saye yt euery persone yt nature hathe prudence called naturall wytte connynge gotten yt persone bryngeth hym praysynge grete excellence yet suche hathe one thou thyselfe hathe sayd yt another hath one gyfte god y• goten longe studyenge yet ben bothe good sooner shall chose naturall wytte without scyence goten thā goten scyence neuertheles vpon preposycyon may many opposycyons founde whiche maye sprynge questyons ynowe one myght say dothe well chose whiche moost auaylable profyte comune nede knowe scyences profyteth synguler persone persones shewynge dothe others sholde naturall wytte sholde haue naturall wytte maye endure durynge lyfe persone hathe dyeth wette dyeth hym scyence goten endureth perpetually euer theym hathe knowe praysynge profyteth vnto many people soo moche teche vnto others maketh bookes vnto theym ben come theyr scyence dyeth may shewe ye ensample arystotle others y• whiche scyences brought ye worl de y• profyteth y• worlde connynge go ten dothe y• prudence without scy ence goten yt men passed yt ben withstandynge yt prudence many dyuers royalmes empyres hathe ben well gouerned dressed yet al thynges ben faylynge gothe men scyence endureth euer yet questyon shall leue vnassoylled determyne others draweth purpose y• strengthynge cyte shall tourne agayne questyon thou hast made knowe yf natural prudence woman whiche thynge answere y• soo thou mayst knowe yt sayd fore thou mayst se generally gouer naunce offyces put yf thou take hede shall seme y• good thou shalte fynde gouerne theyr housholde pouruaye thynges theyr puyssaunce ben comunely moost partye ryght curyous quycke dylygent moche theyr neglygent housbandes thynketh yt grete anoyaunce yt busy moche perteyneth pour uaye saye wolde maystresses wyse thus wolde tourne euyl yt many womē say thē good entente wyse woman spe keth y• epystle salamon whiche y• substaūce purpose wyll say yt foloweth ¶ epystle salamon boke prouerbes ca xliiij shall fynde stronge woman yt say wyse housbande shall faute good praysed ye countre housbande truste th wel yeldeth hym al wel prosperyte tymes seketh pour chaseth wolles vnderstande werke kepe meyny profytable werkes garnysshe hous • ande herselfe put handes busynesse shyp marchaunte yt bereth manere goodes pouruayeth brede gyueth gyftes yt ben wor thy ben counsayllours haboundaunce meetes drynkes spryngeth also seruauntes consydereth value maner bye yt werke wytte hath planted vynes whiche hous holde pouruayed gyrdeth raynes wt strengthe constaunce busynesse ar me ben contynuall good werke seeth busynesse good therfore contynueth moche yt lyght laboure shall neuer quenched darke tyme cometh busyeth herselfe stronge thynges dysprayseth woman workes herselfe worketh stretcheth handes poore feble theyr socoure house pourueyaunce kepte al maner coldnes snowe yt hath gouerne ben clothed double robe maketh herselfe robe sylke purple worshyp renowne housbande worshypped set ye fyrst auncyent men ye erthe maketh cloth lynnen wollen yt selleth clothynge strengthe worshyp ioye perpetuall shal mouthe speketh alway wordes wysedome lawe buxomnesse tongue consydereth prouysyons house eteth brede ydell condycyons chyldren sheweth yt theyr moder werke sheweth goodnesse clene rayment housbande yeldeth praysynges maystresse doughters al thynges thoughe grete dysprayseth false praysynges vayne beaute suche woman shall drede lorde shall praysed shall yelde fruyte werke whi che prayseth place ¶ speketh gay cyryle ca xlv purpose yt epystle salamon sayth wyse woman maye well remembred noble quene gay cyryle lady rome constaunce maryed kynge ye romaynes prudence dede gouernaunce ryght vertuous grete naturall wyt trouthe bounte yt aboue woman praysed ryght grete vyander notable pourueyaū ce thoughe quene myght well leue werke handes yet ye herte alwaye profyte thynge noo tyme ydle alway laboured werke wyse made ye ladyes damoyselles aboute laboure especyall yt serued founde ye maner sorte wolles make fyne clothe dyuers sortes yt occupyed whiche ye tyme ryght honourable thyn ge whiche noble lady place praysed worshypped whiche ye reuerence memory romaynes whiche encreased ryght grete puyssaunce whiche tyme ordeyned maynteyned custo yt weddynge doughters spouse sholde entre fyrst ye house housbande one asked howe sholde named answered gaye gaue vnderstande yt wolde folowe lady dedes werkes puyssaunce ¶ speketh aduyse dydo quene cartage ca xlv • prudence thyselfe hast sayd befo haue aduyse beholdynge vpon thynges one wyll take hande howe yt sholde determy ned yt woman sholde suche respecte aduysed grete matter shall gyue ye yet ensample puyssaunt ladyes fyrst dydo dydo fyrst named elyxa connynge prudence shewed well wer kes shall tell ye founded edyfyed cy te ye lande auffryke named cartage ye whi che lady quene maner yt foundynge gete ye lande possede shewed grete constaunce noblesse vertue without whi che haue grace veray prudence maye ony persone comynge lady fenyce whiche ye last partyes egyp te came ye lande syrye founded buylded dyuers noble townes cytees amonge ye whiche people kynge called agenor ye whiche descended lygnage fader lady dydo whiche named beel kynge fenyce put royalme cypre vnder subieccyon kynge one sone named pygynalyō mayden dydo wt mo chyldren came dethe charged gretely baron yt sholde bere ij chyldren loue trouthe de promyse hym ye kynge deed crowned pygynalyon sone wedded elyxe whiche ryght fayre mayde duke countre whiche grettest ye kynge called acerbe cyte cytens cyteon grete preest temple hercules theyr lawe meruayllous ryche mā wyfe loued moche togyder ledde good lyfe kynge pygynalyon shrewde condycyons cruell moost coueytous persone one myght se coude haue moche wolde coueyte elyxe syster whiche knewe well grete coueytyse also knewe well housbā de grete treasoure grete spekynge rychesse counsaylled aduysed hym sholde kepe hym kynge sholde put goodes secrete place entente kynge sholde take awaye cycyens byleued well counsayle yet kepte well persone awaytes kynge tolde hym kynge made hym slayne daye entente yt myght haue grete treasoures whiche dethe elyxe grete sorowe nere hande deed longe tyme wepynge wayllynge soro wynge pyteously hus bande lorde cursynge cruell brother made hym dye false kynge founde wyle opynyon whiche yt founde lytell nought goodes cytens bare grete rancoure syster thought hydden goodes whiche sawe well yt grete peryll lyfe warned prudence le ue owne countre go then thynge remēbred toke aduyse herselfe vertuous courage yt sholde armed stren gthe constaunce put effecte yt wolde take hande lady knewe well yt kynge welbyloued lordes people ye grete crueltyes extorcyons yt dyde toke certayne lordes cytesyns also ye comune people yt de swere yt sholde holde counsayle suche thyngesas wolde deuyse ryght fayre language began declare enten te moche yt accorded go ther made theyr othe trewe faythfull lady soone myght made redy nauye secretly nyght departed wt al grete treasours foyson people charged gretly maryners employ thē go gretter malyce dyde lady knewe well yt broder soone knewe goynge wolde sende people secretly made fylle grete male grete fardelles thynges noo valewe heuy ben grete treasoure yt entente yt delyuerynge foresayd male fardelles yt broder wolde sende sholde let passe hurte goynge whiche thynge came ye poynte longe gone grete foyson people came ye kynge sewyn ge haue arested lady wel wysely spake sayd wente pylgrymage letted lady sawe y• excusacyon wolde aduayle knewe wel yt wolde nothynge wt haue treasoure sayd yt wolde sende hym good wyll yt knewe wel wolde theyr payne contente ye kyn ge appetyte apease y• kynge ye lady wt sorowfull chere thoughe toke sorowe made delyuered male bagges yt trowed verely ye ne well theyr deuoyre y• sholde brynge ioy full tydynges kynge departed quene without makynge semblaunt yt thou ght goynge soone myght wente longe day nyght yt aryued ye ile cypre refresshed ly tell whyle anone toke shyppes whē done oblacyons vnto ye goddes brought ye preest iouys wyfe housholde dyuyned yt sholde come lady ye partyes phenyce ye whiche sholde leue countre sholde go wt thus wente lefte behynde ye lan de grece lande cecyll ye ryght hande sayled longe ye lande • ulye moche yt aryued ausryke toke ye lande anone came ye people ye countre se y• manere people sawe ye lady people brought plentye vy • ay le lady spake ryght frendly sayd yt grete welthe ye herde say yt coun tre come thyder dwell yf pleased answered yt wolde well ye lady yt made semblaūt yt wolde make grete dwellynge vpon straunge lande requyred thē selle vpon ye see coste moche lande onely ye hyde oxe wolde enclose make dwellynge place people whiche thynge graunted couenauntes pryce sworne bytwene lady whiche shewed wyt grete prudence made take hyde oxe made cutte ye smallest thonges yt myght made knytte thē togyder lengthe made stretche vpon ye grounde aboute y• see coste whiche con teyned meruayllous grete countre ye whiche thynge ye seller meruayllous sore abasshed meruaylled moche ye cauteyles womā yt yet must holde theyr pryce▪ thus lady gate lande auffryke ye sayd fortakynge smyten ye heed horse y• whiche heed ye crye flyght byr de vnderstode theyr dyuynynge y• yt cyte sholde founded sholde tyme come men warre wyse armes lady sente anone aboute seke werkemē opened treasoure made buylde cyte meruayllous grete fayre stronge whiche named cartage towre ye dongeon called byrse whiche say ye hyde oxe begāto buylde cyte herde tydynges broder whiche manaced gretely y• company bycause mocked hym ye treasoure answered ye messangers yt treasoure good fayre yt toke bere broder yt aduenture yt brought toke awaye put stede y• false thynges yt myght well ye vengeaunce ye dethe housbande ye goddes wyl yt yt slewe hym sholde reioyce goodes ther fore haue chaunged manasynge thought helpe goddes sholde defende broder de call yt brought thyder wt sayd yt wolde yt sholde abyde wt agaynst courage ne yt sholde come encombraunce ye whiche yf wolde tourne home agayne y• wolde restore thē theyr laboure sende thē forthe answered one voyce yt wolde lyue dye wtout partynge dayes theyr lyues departed messangers ye lady moche myght busyed perfourme cyte • whē wasal made deyned lawes ye people lyue ryght iustyce thus gouerned notably gret prudēce yt al coūtres wente renowne euery māspake onely grete vertue yt moche hardynesse ye fayre entrepryse yt made grete prudent gouernaūce chaunged name called dydo whiche moche say latyne ui rago y• saye yt hath vertue strengthe man thus lyued gloryously grete whyle longer done fortune ben fauourable often tymes enuyous ben prosperyte dystēpered harde drau ght drynke coude holde contente amonge ye prosperytees aduersytees yt happened tyme lady dou ghter urane yt ryght puyssaunt man grece uesta wyfe whiche ryght rude lytell knowynge ye worlde lady opys ops wedded saturnus y• kyn ge crete whiche broder kyn ge vysyon yt wyfe sholde delyuered mā chylde yt sholde slee hym voyde foresayd destenye ordeyned ye men chyl dren yt quene sholde haue sholde slayne yet yt bothe good euyll shal se euery soule shall take agayne body euery soule shal haue praysynge deserte rychesse shall fayle y• false ymages also y• fyre shal brenne bothe see lande al thynge shal perysshe excepte sayntes loued god shall thynge hydde shall open thynges shall dye shal wepynge sorowful people shal strayne theyr tethe dystres sone y• mone sterres shal lose theyr clerenesse hylles valays shal made euen see y• lande thynges shall brought egalnes trompe heuen shall call mankynde come iugement shall grete drede euery man shal wepe folye shal erthe made newe kynges prynces shal come iuge whiche shall gyue euery man deserte fyre brymstone shall departe frome heuen whiche shall fall helle thynges ben conteyned xxvij verse sybylle made whiche merytes bocace sayth wyse auctoures whiche wryteth holdeth yt ryght wel byloued god ought honoured ony womā ye holy sayn te paradyse woman kepte vyrgy nyte ye dayes lyfe presume yt brought vp clennesse herte euyll tatches fouled vyces borne auc tour say ye tyme destruccyon troye lyued vnto ye tyme tarquyne y• proude called deiphyle lady notwithstandyn ge yt lyued meruayllous grete age vyrgyne lyfe y• grete wysdome poetes fayned yt brought hym comforte woman loued moche whiche called anthony houre nyght come iustynyan luste slepe layde heed louers lappe slepe anthony sawe grete egle come flyen ge ouer whiche payned hym come downe kepe vysage iustynyan fro y• brennynge sone wynges woman whiche wyse vnderstode sygnyfyaunce awaked reasoned hym fayre wordes sayd fayre swete loue haue loued moche loue hym whiche mayster body loue ye knowe wel reason louer wel loued loue ought denye nothynge wolde requyre rewarde maydenhede loue one gyfte whiche thoughe ryght grete shal seme ryght lytell yf ye wyl graunte iustynyā answered loue sholde requyre hym hardely sholde fayle nothynge y• myght graunte sayd anthony loue y• gyfte requyre ye shal emperour y• ye haue dyspraysyng poore loue anthony y• may accompanye wt wyfe sholde emperoure sware al goddes thanked hym hertely token promyse gaue hym rynge gaue anone began saye brynge tydynges certaynly thou shalte emperoure shall shorte tyme depar ted passed longe tyme emperour iustyne assembled hoost go vpon perce sykenesse toke hym thrughe whiche dyed prynces ba ron assembled chose newe emperoure myght wel accorde happened maner dyspyte another chose forgate hy• dydey• myght entre grete subtylte sate trone wt prynces kneled hym began reason sayd y• mayde y• come hym aske ryght reason māy• betrouthed gyuen rynge taken emperoure whiche yet thought woman agaynst whiche mo che accused maketh knowe bet ter frome hense forthe wronge theyr accuser yet maye holde styll comune custome yt renneth amonge men wyse amonge woman comune custome woman chylde themselfe also yt theyr hous bandes ben troubled madame frome whens cometh y• wrothe doughters preiudyce y• sone lesse loue theyr fader moder lesse charge sone ¶ answere dere frende thou demaundest y• cause whens cometh answere certaynly cometh ryght grete symplenesse ygnoraunce troubleth notwithstandynge pryncypal cause moueth therto ye cost theyr goodes yt must vnpurse laye age maryage also dothe mekely theyr faders moders theyr age ought trowe thou shalte fynde thynne sowne thoughe ye fader moder make moche theyr sone theyr goodes wexen myghty ryche theyr fader poore wyll dyspyse hym wyll wrothe shamefull se hym yf theyr fader ryche wyll desyre dethe haue good ¶ suche many whan sone maryed god knoweth gre te coueytyse haue alway drawe ye fader moder wolde recke thou ghe sholde dye hongre myght haue al ye moder abydeth wedo ought comforte staffe berer vp age wyll crye tyll haue drawne yt hath yf wyl gyue ynoughe theyr entente wyl haue conscyence moue plee ayenst suche sone ynowe doughters haply also yet thou take good hede trowe thou shalte fynde sone shrewysshe fader moder doughters yet put case good comunely sayd y• doghters holde better company faders moders sone vysyteth comforteth kepeth theyr sykenes ege cause yt sone trauaylleth vp downe worlde doughters coye holde theym nyghe thou mayste se thyselfe notwithstandynge thy bretherne ryght na turall grete loue gone ye quene hypsytrace ca xiiij howe myght • ny crea ture gretter loue another y• ryght fayre good true hypsytrace hus bāde shewed wel wyfe grete kynge mytrydaces whiche gouerned ye coūtres xxiiij language thoughe kynge myghty puyssaunt romaynes moued ryght harde warre agaynst hym y• tyme yt laboured grete charge y• bataylles yt euer wente good wyfe lefte hym thoughe kynge y• maner barbaryne dyuers concubynes neuerthelesse noble lady alway embraced parfyte loue suche maner yt wyse suffred sholde go without ofte tymes bataylles hym peryl lose royalme aduenture lyfe ayenst y• romaynes sholde go straunge regyon ferre countre passe see destres peryllous forestes wente neuer al way ryght true felawe without departynge loued hym parfyte loue yt thought yt man sholde serue lorde clenly ne well sholde agaynst yt phylosophre theofrastus sayth touchynge matter lady yt knewe yt often tymes kynges prynces haue false seruauntes wherof foloweth false seruyce true louer yt entente yt myght mynystre al necessaryes conuenable thyn ge lorde thoughe yt suffred grete payne wolde alway folowe▪ hym moche suche dede habyte woman conuenable expedyent woman nyghe grete kynge soo noble fyghter batayle sholde sene entente mā sholde seme smyte yelowe here golde whiche apparellynge woman thyn ge ryght well semynge yt spared y• fayre fresshnesse vysage ware helme vnder whiche ofte tymes soylled full • wetynge duste fayre body softe vsed harneys habergyon hosed wt yron precyous rynges ryche ornamē te put parte stede whiche bare handes ax harde speres bowes arowes▪ stretchynge aswerde maner noble quene gouerned strengthe grete loue true thus chaunged tendernes fayre body yonge whiche wonte cheryss hed softely delycately lyued manere stronge armed knyght sayth bocaca wryteth story forsaken frendes noo maner hope yet comforted good wyfe whiche counsaylled hym swetely haue hope better fortune grete trybulacyon payned herselfe hym solace reioyse hym swetnesse y• entente appease ne y• wycked spyrytes whiche lykenesse dyuers fowles flyeth aboute deed bodyes whiche thynge meruaylous bocace sayth doubted pre cepte commaundement kynge▪ creonce whiche cōmaunded made crye vpon sorowfull courage vnderset bodyes nowe one nowe another sekynge hym yt loued moche nowe nowe thus seased tyll lyght lytell bronde offyre helde hande knewe ryght entyerly beloued husbande foūde sought yt cryed hyghe voyce ala ala haue foūde hym yt loued moche wepte grete plente teeres knewe often tymes kyssynge mouthe yt lyfe hym wasshed hym wt teeres al stynkynge often tymes grete cryes wepynges vyctoryes souerayne worshyp waxen olde sore brused noble lady iulye wyfe whiche yonge yet loued hȳ soo grete loue y• ended lyfe straunge aduenture happened day pom pee deuocyon gyue praysynge goddes y• goten noble vyctoryes wolde sa crefyse custome countre beest sacryfyed vpon awter pompe deuocyon helde hym one syde robe soylled blode yssuynge oute wounde beest wherfore pompe dyde robe sente home one seruauntes brynge another clene fresshe happened euyll fortune y• y• bare y• robe mette iulye y• wyfe pompe y• whiche sawe ye robe lorde soyled blode yt knewe wel yt dyuers tymes happe ned rome yt best one wol de renne vpon hym enuye sle hym wherwith supprysed sodaynly sygne sawe certayne byleuynge yt happened soo husbande fortune whiche suche sodayne sorowe toke herte yt wolde longer lyue beynge grete chylde fell flatte erthe pale styffe eyen tourned heed myght noo remedy soo sone put oute drede yt yelded vp spyryte whiche dethe reason ought grete sorowe husbande onely preiudycyable hym y• romaynes also worlde y• tyme yf sone lyued y• grete werre neuer ben y• syth bytwene iulyus cesar pompe y• whiche warre preiudycyable londes worlde ¶ noble lady tyerce emulyene ca xx fayre good tyerce emulyene wyfe prynce scypyon y• fyrste affrycan hated husbande also thoughe olde lady grete prudence ryght vertuous husbande olde yet fayre yonge▪y• notwithstandynge laye bonde woman whiche seruaunt often fell y• worshypfull lady perceyued withstandynge y• herte sorowfull v • ed ye vertue grete vnderstandynge onely y• passyon ialousye dyssymyled wysely y• husbande ne none herde ne uer
