bry tayne lyued late countesse coemen whiche floure youthe fayre aboue ladyes grete goodnesse constaunce dyde ¶ uancyppe wyfe phylosopre socrates capitulo xxj vancyppe ryght noble lady woman grete connynge bounte husbande y• grete phylosophre socrates notwithstandynge grete age grete charge serche tour ne bokes pourchace wyfe softe thynges curyous worshypful woman lefte ne uer loue hym trowed grete thynge excellent vnderstandynge grete vertue hym constaunce hym souerayne loue reuerence whē woman knewe yt husbande condempned ye dethe athene yt blamed yt worshypped ydolles sayd yt one god ought worshyp ped serued noble lady myght haue pa cyence thynge fledde heere hangyn ge aboute chekes full sorowe wepynge betynge palays gate housbande founde hym amonge false iuges whiche hadde taken hym venymous drynke shorten lyfe came y• poynte yt socrates wolde put y• cuppe mou drynke venyme wente hym grete wrathe raced cuppe han de threwe togyder erthe socrates repreued counsayled haue pacy ence comforted myght let hym wyse fro yt dethe sorowed strong ly sayd ha harme losse make iuste man dye wrongefully synfully socrates alway comforted sayd y• better y• sholde dye wrongfully ryghtfully passed sorowe ended herte loued hym mo che lyfe ¶ pompe paulyne wyfe seneke capitulo xxij ryght wyse phylosophre seneke notwithstandynge yt ryght olde al entent studyeng fayled y• well byloued wyfe fayre yonge whiche named pompee paulyne charge yt noble lady serue hym kepe hym pea yt ryght truly derely loued hym whē knewe yt ye tyraūt emperour nero whō ben mayster condempned hym dye drowned bayne fatte yt became herselfe sorowe yt wolde fayne dye husbande wente cryenge many vylanyes tyraunt nero entente yt shol de stretche cruelte vpon also auayled moche sorowed dethe housbande yt lyued longe xp̄ine sayd lady yt spake certes madame wordes hathe remembred drawne mynde many woman fayre yonge ryght perfytely louynge theyr husbandes notwithstandynge yt ryght feble olde tyme haue sene ynowe yt haue loued theyr husbandes perfytely hath borne true loue y• whyle lyued namely y• noble doughter one ye grete baron brytayne yt gyuen maryage y• ryght worshypfull consta ble fraunce syr bertram claquyn whiche notwithstandynge yt ryght lewde shap body olde noble lady beynge floure youthe whiche toke hede grete pryce vertue facyon body loued hym ryght grete loue moche yt lyfe plente sorowe dethe ynowe lyke myght telle whiche lette passe shortuesse tyme answere y• le ue ryght well yet shall tell mo ladyes louynge theyr husbandes ¶ noble sulpyce ca xxiij sulpyce wyfe lentylyus cō sulyennole man rome whome loued grete loue appered sholde condempned iuges rome certay ne thynges whiche blamed sente wretchedly exyle vse lyfe poore ly good lady sulpyce notwithstondynge yt rome ryght grete rychesse myght abyde ease reste loued better folowe hus bande pouerte exyle abyde haboū daunce rychesse without hym renoūced herytage goodes countre dyde moche yt stale away fro moder cosynes whiche kepte cause yt sholde go away vnknowne wede dyde moche yt wente housbande xp̄ine sayd certes madame semeth y• ye say wo men haue sene tyme lyke case suche haue knowne husbandes haue become lyppers conuenyent yt departed fro worlde put syke house theyr good wyues euermore y• wolde leue loued better goo wt serue theyr sykenesse holde true faythe promyse maryage thā byde without theyr housbandes well ease theyr house trowe knowe one yonge fayre good whome housbande suspeccyon suche sykenesse frendes hath warned preched leue company dwell answered dayes lyfe wolde leue hym yf make proued yt ataynte ye sayd maladye whiche cōuenyent yt sake ye worlde yt without fayle wolde go hym cause frendes haue lefte make proffe therof also woman knowe leue named yt aduenture sholde dysplease whiche yt haue housbandes cursed vnordynate lyfe y• fader moder woman wolde yt deed dothe may withdrawe woman theyr shrewde husbandes loue better betē many paynes grete pouerte subieccyon theyr husbandes leue saye theyr frendes ye haue gyuē hym hym shall lyue dye thynges sene daye people consydereth ¶ speketh dyuers ladyes respyted theyr husbandes fro dethe ca xxiiij many woman also wy se sayd grete loue theyr husbandes wyll tell yet ¶ happened yt iason ben coltos gete gol den fleece knyghtes brou ght hym whiche countre grece called menudye lefte theyr owne countre cyte wente dwelle another cyte grece called lacedemonye soo gretely receyued honoured moche theyr auncyent noblesse theyr rychesse maryed moost noblest maydens ye cyte moche waxed ryche mounted worshyp lyfted vp themselfe grete pryde wolde make conspyracyon ayenst soueraynes cyte dyde haue lordeshyp theyr ymagynacyon knowen wherfore put pryson condempned dethe ¶ thynge theyr wyues greate sorowes assembled togyder make theyr sorowes counsayled amonge yf ony way myght founde howe myght delyuer theyr husbandes ende theyr conclusyon nyght sholde araye lewde gownes sholde couer theyr heedes wt mantellesas thoughe wolde know ne suche wyse wente pryson soo moche prayed wepynge gyftes kepers pryson yt wolde suffre go se theyr husbandes wt theyr husbādes gaue theyr lewde gow ne toke gownes yt clothed syth put pryson y• kepers trowed yt woman y• tourned agay ne came daye yt sholde dye kepers brought ye tourment whē sene yt woman eche grete meruayle theyr wyse cauteyle soo gretely praysed cytezynes pyte theyr doughters dyed none se worshypful woman delyuered theyr husbandes fro dethe ¶ xp̄ine speketh dame ryght wysnesayen ste sayth woman kepe noo counsayle answere yt maketh porcya capitulo xxv madame knowe certaynely nowe also haue perceyued grete y• loue trouthe many haue hath theyr husbandes therfore haue grete meruayle language y• renneth comunely amonge men also mayster iohn̄ de meun affermeth strongly romaunce y• rose auctours also dothe man say wyfe maye kepte pryue woman holde theyr pea ¶ answere dere frende thou oughtest knowe woman wyse men whiche yf man haue ony wytte ought well aduyse hym wytte wyfe hathe good nesse saye ony thynge yt wolde haue kepte close therof myght come foly mā knoweth hath good wyfe wyse dy crete nothynge trusty worlde y• moche may comforte man dyscrecy secretenesse commended ony persone yet ye purpose woman louynge theyr husbandes late man rome ryght notable named brutus whiche mary ed gentyl woman named porcya noble porcya doughter chaton lesse whiche neuewe grete chaton foresayd housbande brutus felte wyfe ryght wy se secrete chaste tolde entente cassyen another noble man rome purpose sle iulyus cesar counsayle whiche thynge wyse lady aduysynge grete euyl myght come al puyssaunce counsayled hym contrary warned hym myschyefe myght falle therof myght slepe nyght morowe comen foresayd brutus wente oute chambre goo perfourme entrepryse lady whiche wolde full fayne tourne purpose toke rasoure frome barboure thoughe wolde haue pared nayles lete rasoure falle made thoughe wolde haue taken vp anone smote herselfe ye hande wherfore woman sawe wounded cryed pyteously strongely yt brutus tourned agayne sawe hurte blamed sayd offyce werke rasoure ye barboure answered hym done soo folyly thought done purpose assaye howe myght sle herselfe yf y• entrepryse made sholde tourne hym euyll wolde leue wente anone bytwene hym cassyen slewe iulyus cesar anone exyled brutus slayne notwithstandynge fled rome porcya good wyfe knewe deed sorowe grete forsoke ioye lyfe yt men toke awaye kny ues thynges myght sle folkes sawe wel wolde wen te fyre toke brennynge cole brente dyed waye ended noble lady porcya whiche moost straungest de euer ony dyed ¶ yet matter speketh noble lady curya ca xxvj yet shall tell purpose ayenst yt saye yt woman kepe counsayle alwaye conty nuynge matter grete loue yt many woman haue theyr husbandes curya noble romayne meruayllous fayth constaunce wysdome loue towar de quyntus lucrecyus husbande sayd husbande lyke wyse sholde condempned dethe certayne cryme yt put vpon sholde come know ledge yt one sought iustyfyed happened hym well space flee fere founde wente hyde caues wylde beestes yet durst abyde lucrecyus ye good counsayle wyfe parted neuer chā bre sought came helde hym bytwene armes bedde hyd hym soo wysely neuer perceyued hym hym wysely bytwene ye wal le chambre neuer none • ynye perceyued ne knewe coude well ke pe counsayle grete cautele wysdome yt clothed poore clothes heere hangyn ge aboute chekes al forwepte betynge hā de togyder wente aboute stretes ye temple asked aboute husbande serched yf ony persone knewe husbande become place fled desyre felawe hym exyle myseryes way wysely coude fayne neuer man perceyued saued hym yt comforted housbande full sorowe shortely saye moche dyde moche purchaced hym delyuered hym onely exyle dethe also ¶ yet purpose ca xxvij purpose telle ensamples ayenst say woman kepe noo counsayle truely myght tell ye ynowe thē without nombre let suffyse ye one shall tell yet tyme y• nero tyraunt emperour reygned rome certayne men consydered ryght grete myscheues crueltes ye sayd nero dyde sholde grete welthe profyte ta ke away lyfe fro hym made conspyra cyon ayenst hym aduysed sle hym men repayred al ye house one woman whiche trusted moche spared saye dede theyr conspyracyon happened euenynge tyde aduysed put effecte y• mournynge theyr entrepryse souped sayd wo man kepte wysely fro spekynge whiche mysaduenture yt herde whiche flatter haue grace emperoure wente tolde hym herde say whiche soone departed sayd woman sergeauntes emperoure came ye woman house bycause founde men yt conspyred thus ye dethe ye emperour toke woman ledde ye emperoure whiche enquyred gretely matter coude neuer doo moche gyuynge grete gyftes promyse force tourmentes whiche spared none myght knowe woman men ne yt knewe ony thynge suche matter thus woman meruayllously proued bothe secrete constaunte ¶ proues ayenst say man lewde byleueth counsayle wyfe taketh ony hede therto ca xxviij madame reason vnder stande y• se moche wyt welthe womā mer uayle dyuers men saye yt men ben lewde fooles yt byleue gyueth credence ye counsayle theyr wyues ¶ answere haue sayd wo men wyse yt haue wyues good wyse dothe grete foly byleue thou mayste se haue sayd yf brutus byleued porcy wyfe sleynge iulyus cesar hadde slayne hymselfe ne euyll happened felle entred purpose shall tell dyuers whome hath happened euyll wyse byleued theyr wyues also shall tell dyuers whome hathe well happened byleued theyr wyues yf iulyus cesar whome haue spoken byleued y• ryght wyse good womā whiche many token sene apperynge betokened y• dethe husbande horryble dreme nyght whiche counsayled hym tourne purpose sholde come counsayle yt daye yf come ben slayne also wyse pompe wedded iulye doughter iulyus cesar haue sayd wedded another noble lady named cornelya whiche purpose abouesayd loued hym moche yt none euyll fortune happened hym wolde leue hym also constrayned fle see batayle whiche dyscom fyted iulyus cesar good lady alway hym bare hym company al perylles aryued kyngdome egypte tholomee kynge countre made semblaunte treason ioye comynge sente people hym thoughe sholde receyue hym ioy sle hym whiche people sayd hym sholde entre theyr shyppes sholde leue people entente yt myght brynge theyr vesselles porte lyghtely whē wolde haue entred theyr shyppes good wyse wyfe cornylle counsayled hym y• contrary sholde go ony put people away hym sawe yt wolde byleue counsayle wolde haue gone shyp hym wolde suffre made holden strengthe began sorowe neuer fayled y• dayes lyfe ferre alwaye beholdynge hym sawe traytours murther hym within shyp whiche wolde haue drowned herselfe see yf ben kepte strengthe ¶ also happened myscheuously ector troye y• nyght yt slayne adromatha wyfe ryght meruaylous vysyon yf ector wente batayle morowe yt sholde dye fayle whiche lady affrayed thynge whiche dreme meruaylous prophecy prayed hym ioyned handes vpon knee hym beryng bytwene armes two fayre sone yt day sholde co batayle dyspysed wordes thynkynge euermore semed hym yt sholde reproffe hym counsayle wor de woman sholde leue go ye batayle nother prayer fader moder hadde prayed requyre hym wolde leue wherby happened hym sayd slayne achylles therfore ben bet ter yt byleued ¶ case infynyte ght tell y• men happened full euyl dyuers maners yt dysdeyned byleue y• coūsayle theyr good wyse wyues yf ony euyll come yt dyspyseth theyr counsayles woman ought blamed ¶ speketh yt good comynge byleueth yt counsayle theyr wyues gyueth ensample dyuers ladyes ca xxix whome hathe fortuned well byl • uynge y• counsayle theyr wyues shall tell ye let suffyse proffe soo moche myght say processe sholde without ende lette auayle whiche sayd many maye serue purpose ¶ emperoure iustynyan whome sayd baron hym helde hym felawe loued hym hymselfe called bellyfere whiche ryght worthy knyght emperoure made hym mayster gouernoure cheualry made hym syt table serued hymselfe say also shewed hym many sygnes lo ue baron grete enuye therof soo moche sayd emperour en tended slee hym take empyre vpon hym emperour byleued thynge sone fynde way couertely howe myght make hym dye commaunded sholde go fyght ayenst people called y• uoendres man myght haue better grete strengthe bellyfere vnderstode commaundement knewe well emperour charged hym thynge yf fallen grace benyuolence meruayllously sorowfull myght wente home house wyfe whiche called antonye syster y• empresse sawe husbande lye vpon bedde pale pensyfe eye full teeres grete pyte hym demaunded hym moche grete payne tolde herthe cause sorowe y• lady vnderstode made sēblaunt ryght ioyous comforted hym sayd syr haue ye none thynge dyscomforteth yt vnderstande faythe ihesu cryst yet ryght newe therfore good lady whiche cry sten woman began saye haue ye trust ihesu cryste yt crucyfyed ye shall haue ye hygher hande enemyes ye helpe hym thoughe enuyous wolde noye ye shall soo moche worthynesse ye shall yelde lyers y• saye byleue well dyspyse wordes lette hope god promyse ye shall ouer come well ware y• ye shewe noo maner semblaunt haue ony dyspleasaunce thynge man se sory ryght ioyfull well contente ye shal assem ble hoost hastyest wyse ye maye beware also man knowe porte ye wyll aryue also loke y• ye haue shyppes • owe parte hoost two partes soone ye maye secretly one partye entryn ge auffryke anone renne vpon ene myes shall haue partye youre people shal aryue see hauen tell shall abyde gyue batayle shall entre parte townes cytees shall put theym ye dethe brenne destroy fynde bellyfere byleued well coūsayle wyfe soo dyde wyse man ne lesse yt sayd ordeyned hym waye y• whiche came well passe yt ouercame enemyes put vnder subieccyon toke ye kynge uoendres noble voctory counsayle wytte worshypfull wyfe emperour loued hym better euer dyde ¶ also kynge alexan der despyte wordes ye quene wyfe doughter dayre kynge per se sayd alexander felte em poysoned seruauntes grete soro felte wolde go cast hymselfe ryuere ende lyfe sooner ye good lady yt wente ayenst hym thoughe ryght grete rowe toke hym comforted hym sayd hym yt sholde tourne agayne sholde laye hym bedde wolde speke baron wolde make ordynaunce perteynynge suche prynce sholde grete losynge worshyp yf one myght say ympacyence ouercome hym byleued wyfe counsayle made ordynaunces ¶ speketh grete welthe come worlde euery daye cometh cause woman ca xxx madame se infynyte welthes come ye worlde woman alwaye men say none cometh ¶ answere fayre frende thou mayst se haue sayd longe ago contrary yt saye true man may y• grete welthe yt come worlde woman euery daye cometh haue proued noble ladyes hathe brought ye worl de scyences craftes yf suffyse yt haue sayd y• temporall welthes y• ben come shal tell ye yt spyrytualles howe euery man vnkynde forgeteth yt woman gate paradyse opened v ye vyrgyne mary gretter welthe may one desyre god made man haue sayd may forgete grete welthes moders chyldren woman men worlde praye wolde forgete y• welthes toucheth whens spyrytuall let v beholde olde lawe iewes yf thou wylte beholde hystory moyses whome god ga ue lawe ye iewes wryten thou shalte fyn de yt woman yt holy prophete whome came many grete welthes respyted frome dethe shall telle ¶ tyme iewes y• thraldome y• kynge egypte sholde man borne ebrues y• sholde defende chyldren israell bonda ge happened moyses yt noble duke borne moder whiche durste nourysshe hym constrayned put hy lytell basket put hym ryuere happened god wolde sholde saued y• chermyche doughter kynge pharao sported vpon ryuere tyme ye basket f • ted vpon water whiche anone made take vp saue hadde goten sawe chylde soo fayre noo fayrer myght sene meruaylous grete ioy made nourysshed sayd chylde y• myracle wolde souke woman straū ge lawe made souke nourysshed woman ebrues moyses chosen god age whome god gaue lawe drewe chyldren israell hondes egyptyens passed reede see duke conduytoure ye chyldrē israel thus came grete welthe ye iewes ye cause womā yt saued hym ¶ iudyth noble lady ca xxxj noble lady wydowe iudyth saued people israell frome peryss hynge tyme secon de nabugodonosor sente holophernes duke cheualry vpon iewes conquered lande egypte sayd holophernes grete puyssaunce hadde besyeged iewes cyte also fared soo fowle theym myght abyde longe taken away cōduytes water al theyr vy taylles began fayle nowe ye iewes hope haue power ayenst hym vpon poynte taken hym naced gretely wherfore grete sorowe wente theyr prayer sechynge almyghty god wolde haue pyte people defende theyr ene myes god herde theyr prayer wolde saue mankynde womā wolde saue thē socoure woman cyte iudyth wyse woman whiche yet yonge ryght fayre yet chaste better moche pyte people suche desolacyon prayed god nyght aud daye wolde socoure god enspyred whome grete trust aduysed grete herdynesse nyght commended god departed cyte seruaunt wente moche tyll came hoost holophernes yt made watche ye hoost perceyued grete beaute lyght mone ledde anone holophernes whiche receyued grete ioye yt fayre made sytte hym praysed moche wytte beaute beholdynge gretely embraced loue grete desyre coueted thought otherwyse prayed god alway thought yt wolde helpe perfourme yt wolde ledde holophernes alway forthe wt fayre wor de tyll yt sawe tyme come thyrde parte ye nyght holophernes gyuen souper baron well dronken well chaufed wyne mete myght abyde lenger fro bedde sente good la dy iudyth yt sholde come hym thē tolde wyll tyme sayd nothyn ge contrary entente sayd yt wol pray hym yt ye honeste wolde make voy de pauylyon people sholde goo fyrst bedde wolde come hym fayle aboute mydnyght men slepte thus accorded good lady put payer alway prayenge god yt wolde gy ue hardynes womanly herte ferefull de lyuer people fro ye felle tyraunt iudyth thought yt holophernes slepe came stylly mayden herkened ye dore ye pauylyon vnderstode yt slepte strongely sayd ye lady go hardely god v entred without drede toke ye swer de yt sawe beddes hede drewe hym naked lyfte hym vp strengthe smo te ye heed holophernes without herynge ony body put ye heed lappe soone myght dressed towarde ye cyte moche yt without ony lettynge came gate cryed come come open god v entred man knewe way yt made aduenture morowe hanged heed vpon perche aboue walles people cyte armed manfully ranne vpon theyr enemyes whiche yet theyr beddes toke hede cyte came pauylyon theyr duke make hym aryse hastely founde hym deed al people began sparcle slewe toke yt myght fynde thus ye people god delyuered fro y• handes holophernes iudyth worshypfull lady whiche shall enermore praysed gretely holy scrypture ¶ worshypfull quene hester ca xxxij bi noble wyse lady quene ster god wolde also delyuer people ye bondage kynge assuere kynge assuere greate puyssaunce aboue al kynges dayes posseded many royalmes paynyme helde iewes seruage kynge made seke al royalmes moost noble maydens moost fayre ye best taught chose one amonge al yt myght plea se hym best wyfe amonge others brought hym noble good wyse fayre loued god mayden hester yt ebrue whiche commaunded aboute euer iewes founde sholdde taken quene knewe nothynge yf knowne wolde haue greued euyll yt people sholde euyll entreated neuertheles vncle named mardocheus whiche chyefe iewes made knewe well yt kynge wyndowes y• tournynge towarde chambre kynge thoughe thought hym • awe y• kynge wyndowes anone fell downe knee saluted hym kynge whome pleased humylyte whiche grete pleasure beholde dayes past ye kynge came dyned soo agreable chere yt pleased hym well behelde countenaunce worshyp bounte beaute wolde leue pea sholde aske maner grete gyfte fell downe feete wepynge began say wolde began blowe ryght hyghe blow ynge token entended well ano ne lefte playe ranne towarde ladyes romulus toke kynges doughter gretely smyten loue others wyse toke eche one anone set theyr horse fledde togyder thynge gretely sorowed ladyes y• cyte yt sholde grete man slaughter romulus yssued y• cyte grete hoost quene assembled parlyament al y• ladyes cyte temple whiche ryght wyse good fayre began thus say worshypfull ladyes sabyne ryght dere systers felawes ye kno y• rauysshynge yt done v housbādes y• whiche cause faders frendes ha th moued warre husbandes husbandes ayenst thē may parte hym serued hym well helde hym conten te meruayllously founde neuer good seruaunt woman called herseite sagurat daffynoly saguyr ferant yt wente agayne shyp sagurat daffynoly hym wente moche see tyll woman wyfe tourned home agayne theyr countree lyued togyder longe tyme prosperyte ioye ¶ sheweth howe ryghtwysnesse tolde constaunce lady xp̄ine asked yf true dyuers men saye ben fewe woman true theyr amourouse lyfe therto āswered ryghtwysnes capitulo liij lady ryghtwysenesse tol de thynges ynoughe others whiche leue shortnesse loonce womā grece whiche wolde neuer tourmentes ony man wolde accuse style endytynge make fayre bokes hath suffred longe without sayenge y• contrary many errours wytnessed ayenst dyuers men knewe well yt grete wronge ¶ answere dere frende questyon lyght ynoughe assoyle thou mayst se sayd ye grete vertues ladyes whome haue tolde y• abo ue dyuers werkes dyfferenced one frome another ententyfely occupyed one selfe thynge werke reserued make people good vnderstandynge ye woman praysed ynoughe without wrytynge longnesse tyme passed without gayne saynge thynges cometh well poynte ynoughe ye beholdynge longe worlde longe suffreth god heresyes worlde ayenst holy lawe sholde good shol de suppose men parfyte woman shall folowe ¶ xp̄ine āswered madame nowe let v leue thyse questyons lytel yssuynge termes wherof haue spoken tyll nowe ryght gladly wolde ke demaundes ye purpose yf yt knewe yt sholde noy y• mater thoughe founded vpon lawe kynde cometh attemperynge reason answered vnto dere frende say thou wylte dyscyple yt asketh ye mayster ought reproued thoughe aske yt desyreth knowe madame renneth ye worl de naturall lawe men woman woman men lawe made stablynge peo ple carnal enclynacyon whiche loue eche ryght grete stronge loue one pleasaunt tyme knowe cause ne wherfore suche loue one another fyx ed loue yt comune ynoughe called y• amourous lyfe ye men say comunely yt woman thoughe promyse fe abydynge one place lytell loue ryght subtyll faynte yt cometh lyghtnesse theyr courage amonge auctours y• accuseth yt ouyde boke ye crafte loue gyueth ryght grete charge ouy de sayth others ye wyse haue blamed ynoughe ye woman vpon yt thynge yt put theyr bokes well y• descyuable condycyons theyr wyckednesse yt doo ye comune welthe ye entente aduyse ye mē theyr cauteyles ye better eschewe ye serpent whiche hydde vnder herbe please myne owne lady teche trou th thynge ¶ answere dere frende yt say yt woman desceyuable wote shall say thyselfe hath treated suffycyentely ynoughe matter well ayenst ouyde ayenst others thyne epystle ye god loue epystles vpon romaunce rose vpon poynte yt thou hast touched yt saye yt doo yet comune welthe shall shewe yt nothynge yt cause se reason comune profyte cyte countre comunalte people none thynge one profyte generall welthe y• whiche eche one hath parte thynge yt sholde done profyte sholde called pryuate welthe propre ye comune yet yt shall lesse good yt taken away one gyuen another thynge ought called pryuate welthe propre ryght grete extorcyon made another fauoure partye thou mayst se perceyue clerely yt fauourably preiudyce one parte gryefe sustayne yt spake ye woman aduysynge yt kepe awaytes men yet thynge ryght certayne often tymes yt desceyue woman theyr cauteylous false semblaunt noo doubte yt woman well nombre ye creature erthely men conclu de yt sholde y• comune welthe yt vn derstande ij partes sholde haue spoken well ye woman yt sholde beware men haue done men beware ye woman leue goo questyon folowynge ye yt vnderstande y• woman lytell loue theyr harte sette stabler thā say shall suffy se proue ensample y• haue perceyuered vnto dethe fyrst shal tell y• noble dydo quene cartage whome spo ken aboue grete valoure thyselfe ha touched tymes ¶ speketh dydo quene cartage y• purpose y• loue stable woman ca liiij sayd aboue dydo quene cartage beynge cyte ioy pea reygnynge gloryously come fortune eneas fledde frome troye destruccyon ye du ke capytayne many troyans cast dyuers tempestes theyr shyppes broken theyr vytayles fayled grete losse people desyrous rest ry rouynge y• see busy gete lodgynge aryued y• porte cartage doubte mysta kynge wolde hardy take lōde wt lycence y• quene sente knowe whyder pleased y• noble lady full worshyp worthynes whiche knewe well troyans reputacyon y• tyme ony nacyon worlde y• duke eneas noble blode royall troye gaue hym onely lycence neuer ioy herte ¶ tysbe mayden ca▪ lvj ouyde telleth booke methamorphoseos cyte babylone ij noble ryche cytezynes ryght nyghe neyghboures yt ye walles theyr house yt dwelled ioyned togvder ij men ij chyldren fayre aboue others yt one sone yt named pyra mys yt doughter whiche named tysbe ij chyldren whiche yet without malyce ye age vij yeres loued parfytely togyder yt myght abyde one frome another theyr guyse alwaye yt euery day ryse mornynge togyder take theyr refeccyon theyr faders go play wt chyldren theyr age ye entente yt myght alway togyder al theyr playes one myght se togyder thus endure tyll waxē grete grewe age encreased ye flambes theyr loue moche yt theyr hauntynge perceyued suspeccyon whiche reported moder tysbe whiche toke suche wrathe thynge yt shytte faste chambres sayd wolde kepe well ynoughe fro hauntynge pyramys pryson ryght sorowfull two louers theyr wepynges com playntes ryght pyteous sorowe ryght harde none theym myght se dystresse endured passynge longe whiche made lesse theyr loue ne made nothynge ye slower moche sawe eche alway encreased hete theyr age moche come age xv yeres happened daye fortune wolde thysbe thought alwaye loue wepynge chambre beholdynge walle bytwene y• ij house sayen ge pyteously thou walle harde stone whiche makest departynge bytwene loue yf ony pyte thou woldest cleue sondre entente myght se hym haue desyred moche sayd wordes sawe aduenture corner y• walle cleued whiche perceyued lyght parte dygged clefte pendant gyrdell toole none ye hole encreased moche ye put thrughe pendant entente pyramys sholde perceyue whiche thynge happened token ij louers often tymes assembled speke togyder foresayd hole made theyr pyteous complayntes last constrayned grete loue toke coūsayle wolde stele awaye nyght fro theyr faders moders eche sholde fynde welle vnder whyte mulbery tre wonte playe theyr youthe tysbe whiche loued fyrst come welle abydynge loue beynge aferde lyon herde comynge drynke well fled hyde busshe goynge lete fall whyte couerchefe whi che lyon founde caste vpon entrayles beestes deuoured pyramys came y• tysbe durste come busshe founde couerchefe tysbe whiche perceyued mone lyght charged entraylles trowed verely loue deuoured grete sorowe slewe hymselfe swerde dyen ge tysbe came whiche founde hym poynt token couerchefe y• sawe hym haue hande knewe ye cause y• euyll aduenture wherof suche sorowe y• wolde lyue longer sawe spyry te loue body many gre te • amentacyons made slewe herselfe swerde ¶ good woman hero ca lvij noble yonge woman hero loued moche lesse ye hander dyde tysbe pyramys hander kepe worshyp loued better put hym grete peryll thā sholde blamed hym y• entente y• theyr loue myght endure longer without espyenge ony people toke suche maner se lady often tymes rose nyght bedde entente y• man sholde knowe wente alone arme ye see ryght large whiche called herles passed ouer swymmynge tyll ca castell named habydon y• stode vpon ryuere y• syde y• hero dwelled whiche abode wyndowe longe nyghtes wynter helde bronde fyre wyndo entente y• sholde come ryght way thyder ij louers contynued lyfe many yeres tyll fortune enuye theyr solacyous lyfe thought trouble theym happened tyme wynter y• woodnesse y• see ryuere full tempest passynge depe peryllous whiche tempest durynge longe without seasynge y• thought ryght longe y• one se whiche ryght noyous ij louers gretely complayned y• wynde tempest endured longe last hander whome grete desyre chased y• sawe nyght bronde ye wyndowe y• hero helde semed hym y• called hym thought grete cowardyse y• put hym peryll wente drede whiche doubted hym wolde fayne defende hȳ y• sholde go put hym suche peryll yf myght notwithstandynge helde y• bronde aduenture teche hym ryght way yf wolde nedes thus happened vnhap py aduenture y• hander put hymselfe ryuere myght stryue agaynst flode y• wa ter whiche bare hym soo ferre must nedes drowne good hero herte gaue happened seased neuer wepynge ye clere day appered y• slepte wente agay ne y• wyndowe ben nyght sawe ye body loue flete vpon wa ter nyghe ye brynke y• wolde lyue longe caste ye see dyde moche y• • oke loue armes dyed thus perysshed ¶ sysmonde doughter prynce salerne ca lviij bocace telleth y• boke cent nou uelles y• prynce salerne named cancre fayre doughter ryght gentyll courtoys whiche named sysmonde loued doughter soo grete loue grete payne wolde accorde vnto styrynge lordes marye erle champayne sholde abyde longe maryage erle dyed ye fader toke home agayne hym thynkynge neuer marye agayne lady whiche nourysshed tenderly ryght fayre floure youthe whiche yt knewe wyll fader sholde ryed agayne wente aduysed amonge seruauntes fader squyer whiche aboue al others thoughe grete foy son knyghtes gentyll men semed fayre good worthy loued moche thought passe youthe ioy ously take pleasaūce longe tyme wolde dyscouer thynge behelde euery day sate faders table maner coun tenaunce condycyons squyer whiche named guyscart moche day day semed parfyte amonge thyn ge whiche called hym day sayd hym manere guyscart fayre frende trust haue bounte beaute wysdome counsayleth dyscouer dyuers thynges toucheth ryght secrete whiche wolde tell none body wolde yt tell haue trouthe shal neuer opened guyscart swered madame nede doubte shall nothynge knowne ye tell assure trouthe sayd sysmonde hym guyscarte knowe trouthe yt pleasaunce gentylman loue wylloue may well speke hym whome sende hym wyll wolde ye meane loues nowe beholde yf haue grete truste aboue others wyll put myne honoure handes set hym knee sayd madame knowe wel ye haue su che wytte goodnesse ye wolde thynge vnconuenable soo thanke ryght mekely ye trust another nowe cōmaunde good pleasure seruaunt shall obey power serue hym yf knewe whiche yt happy haue loue lady grete worthynesse ye certes hath fayled noble loue sysmonde yt wyll proue hym herde hym speke wysely thē toke hym hande sayd frende guyscart knowe thou arte haue chosen myne one ly loue wyll take pleasaun ce semeth noblesse thy courage good maners whiche thou arte full yel deth worthy haue hyghe loue yonge man grete ioye thynge thanked ryght humbly shortely say longe tyme con tynued theyr loue without ye ony tydynges felte therof fortune enuyous theyr lace wolde longer suffre ij louers ioy tourned theyr dysporte grete bytter sorowe meruaylous aduenture fortuned somers day yt sysmonde dysported gar dyne maydens yt houre fader none welthe sawe wen te alone chambre dysporte hym wt founde ye wyndowes shytte curteynes bedde drawne body trowed ben slepe wolde awake layde hym lytell couche slepte strongly sysmonde thought yt ben longe ynoughe ye gardyne wente chambre layde bedde slepe woman voyded shytte dore vpon perceyuynge yt fader ony sawe selfe alone rose bedde wente seke guyscart whiche one wardrobe brought hym chambre de uysed bytwene two within curteyns yt trowed yt alone prynce awoke vnderstode yt man doughter grete sorowe ye thynge yt payne consyderacyon yt sholde dyshonoure doughter myght kepe hym▪but de parted neuerthelesse suffred vnderstode wel dyde moche yt lepte chambre knowynge hym two louers ben ynoughe togyder guyscarte departed prynce made watche vpon hym anone made hym ta ken prysoned hym wente doughter beynge alone ye chambre ye eyesfull teeres grete sorowe began saye ¶ sygysmonde trowed haue y• dou ghter aboue woman fayre chaste wyse▪but moche y• ouercome say thou ghe trowed contrary yf sene myne eye nothynge sholde haue made byleue thou sup prysed wt loue ony man▪but ben thyne housbande yt certayne ye sorowe therof shall tourment myne age lytell tyme yt haue lyue whiche en grudgeth moost wrathe y• trowed y• noble courage ony woman bor ne se well contrary y• thou hast taken one ye leest myne housholde yf thou wolde haue done suche thynge thou ghtest haue founde noblesse worshyp courte thou toke guyscart whome trowe yelde sorowe yt haue cause wolde yt thou knowe shall make hym dye wolde yf myght destroy fro myne herte loue yt haue ye gretter euer fader doughter whiche tourneth fro sysmonde vnderstode thynge fader cō dēpned hym deth yt loued moche sorowfull wolde fayne dye yt houre yet ryght stable courage constaunte chere wt castynge ony teeres eye thoughe dysposed lyue longer āswered thus fader syth fortune hathe made yt knowne whiche wolde fayne haue couered haue noo nede make noo request excepte yf wyste aske remyssyon lyfe hym ye manace dethe wolde bese che take myne leue yt aske pardon ye wolde hym ye saye wolde aske wyll noo longer lyue moche make certayne dethe ye shall sle thynge moueth grete wrathe ayenst v haue ye cause take vnto owne blame ye fless haue ye engendred doughter fless stone yron ye ought thynke thoughe ye olde howe grete heuynesse youthe lyuynge delyces ease pryckynges whiche passe syth sawe ye thought neuer mary agayne felynge yonge prycked lustynesse fell loue gentylman without cause ne without grete delyberacyon consented accorded myne herte desyred yet aduysed well condycy ons hym parfyte vertues ony courte ye may knowe selfe whiche haue nourysshed hym thynge noblesse vertues cometh fless blode whiche donge ye haue cause saye haue taken leest noble courte thus ye haue cause wrathe towarde v owne blame cōsydered yf ye wyll take grete punysshment hym trespace perteyneth taken sholde taken wronge synne ryght yt haue whiche styred hym therto whiche thought ought haue certes sholde haue ben moche herte vylayne haue refused lady suche parentage ought ye employe trespace vpon hym vpon prynce departed sysmonde yet appeased warde guyscart mornynge made hym slayne commaunded herte sholde taken body whiche herte y• fader put ryght ryche cuppe golde secremessagere sent vnto doughter sholde say sent presente enioy thynge yt loued moost messagere came sysmonde made present sayd yt charged therwith toke cuppe opened anone knewe aduenture thoughe sorowe inestymable dysmayed hyghe courage made answere hym wyse without chaū gynge chere sayenge frende say y• prynce one thynge perceyue well yt noble herte hathe gyuen suche sepulture perteyneth hym golde precyous stone ought haue thā stouped ouer cuppe kyssed herte sayenge pyteously ha ryght swete herte herboure pleasure cursed cruelte maketh see plyte ye alwaye present myne herte veray eyen thought hast thou passed course thy noble lyfe dyuerse fortune yet thou hast suche asepul ture thyne enemye thy worthynesse hath deserued pertayneth well myn offyce thou wasshed bayned teeres thou loued moche thou shalte fayle therof yt thy soule shal longe without myne reason yt shall make ye companye short tyme yet maulgre fortune hath cōtrarye come moche wele nowe cruell fader bath sent y• thentent yt thou worshypped speke dye soule maye se thyn desyre companye aboue thynge knowe well yt thy spyryte desyreth myne suche wordes others ynowe sayd sysinonde pyteous ony persone harde ought haue grete pyte depely wepte semed y• ij welles hede yt ran wtout ceasynge y• cup wtout makynge noyse crye wt alowe voyce kyssynge alwaye y• herte lady gentylwomen y• grete meruayle thynge knewe nothynge y• aduenre ne cause y• grete sorowe wept pytye payned recō forte auayled vayne asked moost pryue woman cause sorowe ouercome wt meruayllous sorowe whan wepte ynough sayd ryght welbyloued herte haue done al myne ossyce longed y• nowe resteth nought doo sende soule make companye thyne wt wordes lyfte vp opened almarye toke boxe put venymous herbes dyssolue water haue redy whan cause happed cast y• water cuppe herte without ony maner drede dranke layde done vpō bed abydyn ge dethe holdynge y• cup alwaye ryght stratly whan y• woman sawe body chaūge sygnes dethe sorowynge meruayllously cursed y• fader whiche gone lytell whyle dysporte hym came houre venym gan stretche aboute vaynes ful sorowe ye case yt happed repentynge hym yt done bygan speke swete wor de trowyng haue recōforted makynge gre te sorowe doughter āswered hȳ cancre reser ue thy teeres tyl nother tyme nede thē desyre thē yu resemblest ye mad mā yt slewe mā wepte tor better yt yu haddest let thy douzter lyue plesaūce secretly louyng mā thā se hard deth thy cruelte thy grete sorowe whiche dethe shall make thynge secrete appere openly myght speke herte brake holdynge cuppe ryght straytely handes anone ye fader dyed sorowe thus ended sysmonde doughter prynce salerne ¶ lyzabeth louers ca lix also bocace telleth saydbooke cent nouuelles cyte messyne italy yonge woman named lyzabeth ye whiche iij bretherne theyr coueytousnes taryed maryenge factoure gouernoure theyr busyness ryght fayre goodly yonge man whiche theyr fader nourysshed youthe ¶ happened contynuell frequentacyon yt bytwene loued eche loue contynued whyle ryght ioyously last bretherne perceyued wolde make grete noyse dyshonourynge theyr syster aduysed sle hym dede ledde yonge man whiche named laurence vnto manere theues come thyder hym gardyne slewe hym buryed hym amonge tree came home agayne theyr house made byleue yt sente laurence ferre another cou • theyr message lyzabeth whiche loued laurence gre te loue nothynge hertes ease bycause lost ye presence loue herte gaue straungely matter moche yt tyme cō strayned ryght loue myght suffre noo longer yt • ked one bretherne yt laurence taryed longe y• whiche broder answered ryght tyersly sayd perteyneth ye knowe ly zabeth perceyued certaynly y• slayne lau rence ye whiche made meruaylous sorowe alone wepte y• nyght ryght depely wtout takynge ony maner rest cō playnynge hym yt loued moche ther became ryght syke ye whiche sykenesse requyred bretherne yt wolde let go dysporte theyr maner wtout cyte lytel whyle graunted wente thyder whome herte gaue ad uenture wente alone ye gardyne laurence lay deed lokynge aboute sawe ye body buryed raysynge newe erthe dygged ye erthe wt pycoys yt founde moche tyll founde y• body embrasynge ye body grete dystresse made sorowe measure moche knewe myght longe fere sholde perceyued toke ye body ye erthe toke heed loue yt bretherne smyten knytted couerchefe buryed one grete pottes wheron vse set herbes plantes herbe aboue swete ly smellynge yt called basylycon wt potte tourned home house agayne potte grete cherete yt coude parte put one chambre wyndowes ayre watered none water teeres eyen nyght daye thynge endured lytell whyle men saye woman forgeteth lyghtly semed yt sorowe encreased day daye thus basylycon waxen fayre grete fatnesse erthe tell shortely moche ledde lyfe vpon ye potte yt happened yt neyghboures perceyued howe wepte without seasynge wyndowe vpon potte tolde bre therne meruayle sorowe gretely abasshed myght ny ght stale awaye potte wherof mornyn ge began sprynge newe noyaunce whē founde potte grace requy red yt myght haue potte agayne wol de quyte thoughe sholde gyue par te goodes sayd pyteously complaynynge ala houre brought moder forthe worlde cruel bretherne y• whiche hateth symple pleasaūce wyll leue lytell poore potte basylycon whiche cost nought yelde agayne aske nothynge elles maryage dowry ala grete ye desyre thus lete passe soro neuer seased moche yt layde bed sore syke whiche sykenesse euer one offred set ne ioye ye worlde onely potte thus dyed pyteously thynke yt thynge le synge made songe ye complaynte geney • womā pot whiche synge yet shall tell ye sholde holde ye longe yf tolde ye hystoryes woman suche maner loue taken whiche haue loued ryght grete loue ¶ another also telleth boca ce whome ye housbande made eate ye herte loue whiche neuer ete dyde ye lady fayllee whiche loued chastelayne coussy grete loue also soude trystram tyamere whiche loued hercules moche yt slewe herselfe whē deed dou bte y• ryght grete loue cōstaunte womā setteth herte thoughe yt womē lyght ¶ pyteous ensamples ynowe others yt myght tell ought ye cause moue y• courage wo men put peryllous see dampnable lewde loue alway ende therof grete preiudyce grefe body goodes dyshonoure y• soule whiche shalldo wyse womē whiche good wyt eschewe gyue audyence thē whiche wt seasynge trauaylleth thē deceyue theym suche case ¶ iuno dyuers ladyes renowne ca lx nowe haue tolde y• grete foyson ladyes whiche y• hystoryes maketh mencyon saye processe sholde infynyte whiche haue taken honde suttyseth without brynge forth wytnessynge saye contrary y• thou hast purposed dyuers men say wyl tell conclusyon hathe ben y• worlde gretely praysed dyuers accydētes thā grete vertues ¶ iuno doughter sa turnus opys sayenges poetes y• erroure paynymes gretely praysed abo ue woman yt lawe good fortune ony excellence syster iupyter maryed vnto hym whome called souerayne god grete rychesse fortune whiche lyued habounded housbande reputed goddesse rychesse madde people byleued y• stature dethe better fortuned graunted also y• cōforte y• ryghtes maryage helpe woman recouered praynge made temple aboute awters preestes playes sacrefyses thus lōge worshyp ped grekes cartage brought rome put y• capytole celle iupyter housbande worshypped romaynes y• lordes worlde many dyuers cerymonyes longe tyme ¶ also europe yt doughter agenor kynge phenyce also gretely praysed iupyter whiche loued named thyrde parte y• worlde name knowe name dyuers woman hathe ben dyuers landes cytees townes named englonde woman called angle others ¶ iocasta quene thebe praysed grete infortune mysaduenture wed ded owne sone yt slayne owne fader wherof none theym bothe knewe sawe dyspayred knewe y• aduenture sawe hym slayne bytwene two sone yt ¶ also meduse bargon praysed grete beaute doughter ryche kynge porce y• royalme ryght haboundauntly closed y• see duse auncyent hystoryes sayth soo meruayllous beaute onely passed woman meruayllous thynge aboue nature countenaunce pleasaunt beaute body vysage yelowe heeres longe thredes golde cryspe drewe euery mortall creature yt behelde unmouable people therfore fable fayneth became stone ¶ helayne wyfe menelans kynge lacedemoyne doughter tyndarus kynge ceballe leyda wyfe gretely renowmed grete beaute happened bycause rauyss hynge parys made whiche y• cause whiche troye destroyed quene thoughe sayd beaute others hystoryes affermeth fayrest womā euer borne moder therfore poetes saye engendred iupyter grete god ¶ also polexene meke doughter kynge pryamus also fayre mayde made mencyon ony hystore y• ryght stable constaunte courage shewed receyuynge deth without vysege • heeded vpon tombe achylles sayd agreable dye ledde seruage others ynowe myght tell y• whi che leue shortenesse ¶ speketh xp̄ine ryghtwysnesse answe reth ayenst woman drawe mē theyr gaynesse ca lxj ixp̄ine sayd thus madame truely y• purpose aboue sayd peryllous lyfe foly loue y• se truely ought eschewed woman haue ony vnderstandynge soo moche preiudyable grete blame gyuen delyte gay theyr araye clothynge saye drawe mē theyr loue ¶ answere dere loue shall excuse curyous quaynte theyr aray without fayle vyce lytell ne quayntenesse estate perteyneth euery persone bere without blame y• whi che excuse euyll entente none charge gyue greter blame ne affermeth suche woman yt one seeth fresshe gaye say certaynely co meth woman bycause loue cometh many well men woman ryght good condycyón naturall inclynacyon delyte theym fresshenesse fayre habytes ryche clennesse profytable thynges yf come kynde herde eschewe howe sholde vertuous ¶ wryten appostle saynt barthylme whiche ryght grete gentyll man notwithstandynge sauyoure cryste ihesu preched teched strongly pouerte lymplenesse maner thynges yet blessyd apostle lyfe ware clothes sylke frenged aboute golde precyous stone co meth hym kynde rychely arayed y• whiche comunely curyous thynge full pryde yet synned wyll say cause lorde suffred martyr dome lefte skynne slayne se thynges tell showe mā ought iuge another conscyence haby te ne araye perteyneth onely god iuge creature vpon shall tell ensamples ¶ claudyne woman rome ca lxij also bocace ualere telleth y• clau dyne whiche noble lady rome delyted gretely fayr • clothynges delycate yt modelycatyfe ladyes rome presumed shrewdely ayenst ayenst chastyte y• preiudyce good name happened xv yere seconde batayle aufryke ymage pyssemonde moder ye goddes opynyon ben borne fro rome assembled noble ladyes rome go mete ymage whiche put shyp vpon tybre y• maryners myght aryue porte theyr strength claudyne whiche knewe well yt mysbylened wronge fresshnesse kneled ymage made prayer hyghe sayenge goddesse truely knewe chastyte hole cor rupte wolde gyue grace alone myght drawe shyp hauen trustynge clennesse toke gyrdell boun de sterne shyp atter drewe shyp ryuayle lyghtly thoughe maryners worlde ben euery body meruaylled therof haue tolde y• ensample thynge wene y• ymage foles myscreauntes call goddesse yt myght lyfte vp prayer claudyne haue tolde shewe gaye lefte moche chaste shewed trouthe chastyte courable whiche helped goddesse ¶ howe lye vpon womē mo che thoughe delyte fayre clothynge araye ca lxiij woman wolde byloued payne y• cause gaye nyce curyous shall proue yt encheson maketh sooner ne better loued wyse men worshyp sooner better ben vertuous woman honest symple loued loue worshyp moost iolyest fayrest one myght answere thus syth woman drawe men theym theyr vertue honeste better fewer good woman y• reason sholde nought worth good profytable thynges ought lefte tolde encrease thoughe foles abuse euery mā ought deuoyre wel doynge thoughe fortune contrary yt soo many woman ben loued theyr vertues honeste shall shewe ensamples fyrst dyuers sayn te paradyse myght tell couey ted men theyr honeste ¶ lucresse spake aboue whiche rauysshed grete honeste cause tarquyne lo ued beaute hous bā de one soupere tarquyne whiche rauysshed dyuers knyghtes theym began speke theyr wyues euery mā sayd best knowe ye trouthe proue whiche • theyr wyues moost worthy praysed euery man wente horse backe wente theyr house thoughe yt founde occupyed moost honest offyces werke y• mo • e reputacyon wherof fortuned yt lucresse amonge founde y• moost honestly occupyed ryght wyse good womā clothed symple gowne amonge maydens womē werkyngein wulles spekynge ver tuous thynges thyder came y• sayd tarquyne sone y• kynge hous bade whiche behol dynge grete honeste symple countenaūce styll manere amerous yt cau • ed hȳ folye dyde • ter ¶ quene blaunche moder saynt lewes • good woman loued theyr vertues capitulo lxiiij wyse loued gre te vnderstandynge wysdome vertue bounte ryght noble quene blaūche moder saynt lewes y• erle chāpayne • standynge passed ye floure youthe ble erle herynge y• quene speke hym wt wyse wordes begon warre agaynst y• sayd sayd saynt lewes good lady spake hym sayenge ought cō syderynge welthes sone done hym erle behelde grete entent meruay lynge hym grete goodnesse vertue ye whiche strongely vndertaken wt loue yt wyst say ne durst neuer warre ayenst hym knewe wel y• moche welthe vertue also yt coude neuer otherwyse accorde wt hym suffred fro houre many trouble lewde desyres cōstrayned hym yet answered hym doubted sholde neuer make warre kynge wolde incertayne herte body yt euer submytted commaundement soo loued hym lyfe lefte lytell wanhope myght come loue made louely complayntes dyttyes praysynge gretely lady whiche goodly dyttyes made put musyeyen set songe ryght delectably halle prouynce also troyes made wryte yet appere many place thus myght tell many ¶ xp̄ine answered madame purpose lyke case haue sene experyence knowe many vertuous woman haue confessed complaynynge pleasaunce toke haue ben requyred syth y• tyme y• theyr grete beaute youthe hath ben past▪ theyr grete f • oure wherof sayd ala wyll ye say men seynge ony countenaunce foly y• whiche haue coloure cause thynke accorde grete foly perceyue nowe open ly y• ye saye grete welthe hathe ben cause make loue well contrary y• opyupon dyuers folke yt say good woman wolde chaste shall ne uer woman lyst coueyted quyred ¶ xp̄ine asketh ryght wysnes answereth ayenst saye woman nature ben scarse capitulo lxv replye myne owne lady questyons ben well assoyled semeth ye ha ue ynoughe proued false euyll say enges yt many men saye vpon woman also amonge vyces womē saye yt auaryce naturall thynge appereth ye saye ¶ swere dere doughter tell certaynly yt auaryce naturall woman men yf lesse god knoweth thou mayst se y• couetysenesse dyuers men moche harme done worl de lytell couetysenesse woman haue sayd y• fole knoweth better lytell trespace neyghboure dothe grete cryme hymselfe one sethe often tymes y• woman delyte louynge spynne carde suche thyngesmē call couetyse promyse yt ben grete foyson yf wherof wolde scarse ne couetouse yt sholde theyr worshyp poore men holde comunely theyr wynes strayte yt must nedes kepe haue wote well lyght thynge haue ben people yt calleth woman scarse yt haue ryed full large wastours theyr goodes poore woman yt knewe well yt theyr housbandes haue spended lewdely yt sholde fynde theyr housholde theyr chyldren dare compare chere maye holde speke theyr housbandes coūsayle lesse de spence suche thynges coueytyse ne scar senesse sygne ryght grete prudence suche debate one may se often tymes maryages yt suche counsayllynge pleaseth men yt gyue blame woman yt ought prayse yt true vyce auaryce wyll say appereth almesse ry ght good wyll dayly god knoweth howe many prysoners londe y• sara • yns howe many nedy gentylmen others haue ben ben dayes lowe worlde comforted socoured woman theyr goodes ¶ ladyes rome scarse ty y• cyte gretely greued warre whiche y• comune treasoure y• towne wasted spended men armes wherof grete sorowe y• romaynes fynde way haue syluer put forth armye whiche force ryght necessary la dye theyr owne fre wyll also wydowes assembled brought theyr iewelles al without sparynge ony thynge y• prynces rome freely toke y• whi che thynge ladyes gretely worshypfull ryche woman buyse paulyne whiche y• londe puyl le tyme yt hanyball gre ued moche romaynes fyre yren yt despoyled almost italy men goodes happened yt y• grete dyscomfyture cane wherof curtoys ly berall myght tell ynoughe ¶ also sekynge ferther hystoryes well largesse ladyes myght tell ynoughe ne lyberalyte grete noble lady de la ryuere named margarete whiche yet lyue somtyme wyfe lorde burell lorde de la ryuere fyrste chambrelayne wyse kynge charles lady yt alwaye wyse worshypfull well manered happened tyme amonge others yt beynge grete feest grete foyson noble ladyes knyghtes gentylmen grete apparayle noble lady whiche fayre yonge behelde y• noble cheualry thought che amonge others ryght notable knyght grete worshyp lyuynge called syr emenyon de pomyners lady lefte moche yt goodly man haue remem braunce hym bycause worthynesse bounte thought y• fayrer araye myght company notable men good fame thoughe olde asked gretely syr emenyon y• assemble tolde pryson castell parys fyue hon dred frankes whiche boūde vyage dyde armes dyde ofte tymes ha sayd noble lady shame ye realme suffre suche man houre pryson dette toke chapellet golde vpon hede ryght ryche fayre put vpon stede chapellet per uencle toke certayne messagere sayd go put chapellet plegge oweth delyuered anoue come heder whiche thynge done whi che gretely praysed ¶ pryncesses ladyes fraūce ca lxvij xp̄ine sayd thus madame sythe ye haue remēbred lady tyme entred pourse ladyes fraunce bydynge coūtre pray please saye som ye seme ought sayd yfye thynke yt good maye harboured cyte whe refore ought forgotten thoughe straungers answere xp̄ine answere certaynely se many thē ryght vertuous pleaseth wel y• cytezeynes fyrst shall refused noble quene fraunce isabell debauere nowe grace god reygnynge neuer founde cruelte extorcyon ne none euyl vyce alway good loue benygnyte subiectes ¶ ne ought gretely praysed y• fayre yonge good wyse duchesse berry wyfe duke iohn̄ late sone kynge iohn̄ fraū ce broder y• wyse kynge charles y• whiche noble duchesse bare herselfe wysely chaste floure youthe y• y• worlde praysed grete vertue sholde say y• y• duchesse orlyaunce wyfe lewes sone charles y• wyse kynge fraūce late doughter ye duke myllayne whiche prudent lady ye myght tell y• stronge constaūte courage grete loue lorde aduysed gouernaunce iust euery mā wyse behauoure ¶ saye y• duchesse burgoyne wyfe duke iohn̄ sone phylyp late sone kynge iohn̄ fraūce ryght vertuous true lorde benygne herte countenaunce good cō dycyons without ony vyce ¶ countesse cleremount doughter y• duke berry aboue sayd fyrst wyfe maryed y• erle cleremount sone y• duke burbon abydynge y• duchy y• tale suche y• perteyneth euery hygh prȳcesse y• gret loue lorde wel manered thynges wyse vertues appe red lyke woman wyse gyuen vnto men hath gyuen vnto wo men vnderstande theyr yonge tendre age constaunte stronge sufferynge horryble martyrdomes y• holy lawe whiche ben crowned glorye whome fayre lyuesben good ensample euery euery woman aboue othher wysdome ther fore shall y• superlatyue degre cyte fyrst ryght excellent y• blessyd katheryn whiche doughter kynge costes alexā dre blessyd vyrgyn lefte heyre fader age xviij yeres notably gouerned herytage crystē wo mā gyuen god refusynge marya ge happened cyte alexandre come y• emperour maxencyus whiche day grete solempnyte goddes made aray grete appareyle make solempne sacryfyse katheryne beynge palays herde noyse beestes yt arayed sacryfyse grete noyse instrumentes sente knowe reported ye emperour temple sacrefyse anone wente began correcte y• em peroure yt erroure many wyse wordes grete clerke lerned scyences began proue good reason phylosophye yt one god maker thynges yt ought worshypped none yt emperour herde mayden whiche ble grete auctoryte thus speke whiche yt fayre admeruaylled wyste say entended beholde sen te al aboute seke phylosophres ye londe egypte came hym l phylosophres whiche helde thē ryght euyll contente knewe cause wherfore brought thy der sayd lytell wytte moued trauayle frome farre coutrees dyspute mayden telle shortely y• day theyr dysputac yon come blessyd katheryne ledde theym argumentes ouercome coude assoyle questyons y• whiche y• emperoure pa synge wrothe aduayled thynge grace god holy wor de vyrgyne conuerted confessed name ihesu cryst whiche despyte emperoure made brente holy mayden conforted theyr martyrdome assured receyued perpetuall glory prayed god wolde kepe veray faythe put y• nombre blessyd martyr suche myracle god shewed y• fyre neuer hurte theyr bodyes ne theyr clothes bode al hole fyre done wtout losynge ony heere theyr heedes semed lyue tyraunte maxencyus whiche gretely coueyted holy vyrgyne katheryne beaute began flatter y• sholde tourne wyll sawe aduayled nothynge tourned hym manasynges tour mented made beten cruelly put pryson without vysytynge ony per sone y• space xij dayes without mete drynke trowynge haue made dye hongre aungelles lorde whiche comforted xij dayes brou ght emperoure sawe fresshe hole trowed ben vysyted commaunded kepers pryson tourmented kathe ryne whiche pyte affermed comforte saue onely heuen em peroure wyst harde tourmentes ght make tourment counsayle prouoste lete make wheles full rasoures whiche tourned one ayenst another someuer myddes al cutte bytwene wheles made put saynt katheryne naked whiche alwaye emperoure dyde wente vysyted holy vyrgyne pryson prayed wolde pray god whiche despyte y• emperoure made tourmente wyfe drawe pappes vyrgyne sayd doubte ye y• tourmentes noble quene daye thou shalte receyued ioye without ende emperoure made wyfe heeded grete multytude people conuerted emperoure requyred katheryn wolde wyfe sawe refusynge petycyons wente gaue sentence sholde b • heeded made prayer praynge membraunce passyon theym called name theyr trybulacyons god myght theyr helpe socoure voyce came fro heuen whiche sayd yt prayer herde soo made ende martyrdome stede blode ranne mylke body y• aungelles toke holy body bare ye moun te synay whiche xx dayes iourney fro then buryed whiche tombe god hath done many myracles whiche let passe shortenesse tombe renneth oyle whiche heleth many syke men god anone punysshed emperoure ryght hor rybly ¶ saynt margarete ca iiij shall forgete also ye blessyd vyr gyne saynt margarete whome y• legende knowne full well howe borne antyoche noble kynrede introducte y• faythe whē yonge nouryse whome ryght humbly wente euery daye kepe shepe wherof happened y• olybryus whiche stewarde emperoure sawe goynge coueyted sente fetche wolde consente wyll tolde hym crysten wo man made strongly tourmented beten prysoned whiche pryson y• felte tempted requyred myght se hym vysybly soo moche euyll pourchased came horryble serpente whiche gretely made aferde swalowed made sygne crosse anone ser pente brake sawe corner pryson blacke fygure man ethyope margarete wente boldely coniured hym couched vnder feete sette feete vpon throte cryed hygh voyce mercy pryson fulfylled clerenesse margarete comforted aun gelles tourmented agayne iuge whiche sawe ammonycyons aduayled hym made tourmented aungelles god came brake tour mentes vyrgyne lepte awaye hole grete foyson people cōuerted false tyraunte sawe ordeyned y• heeded made oryson fyrste prayed vnto almyghty god theym remembred passyon prayed vnto theyr trybulacyens woman grete chylde almyghty god wolde grauute vnto theyr petycyon ye aungell god came tolde prayer herde sholde go name god receyue palme vyctory stretched forthe necke heeded aungelles bare soule heuen ¶ false olybryus also made tourmente holy vyrgyne named regyne whiche ryght yon ge age xv yeres wolde accorde hym conuerted moche peo ple holy prechynge ¶ holy vyrgyne saynt luce ca v biessyd saynt luce whiche borne rome ought forgeten letanye ye whiche rauysshed ye kynge aceya barbary co • n tre trowed haue defouled vertue god began preche vnto hym yt meruaylled wytte lefte sayd yt goddesse helde grete worshyp reuerence palays ryght reuerent ly establysshed dwellynge meyny ordeyned man sholde repayre thyder hurte trouble without seasynge fastynges orysons ledde ryght holy lyfe prayenge hoost▪ yt myght please god enlumyne hym ly ght holy faythe hoost asked counsayle doynges toke wel euer counsayled hym wente werre prayed wolde praye god hym blessyd hym ca agayne ouercomer enemyes wherfore wolde worshyp goddesse wolde haue made buylde temple sayd sholde beware therof one god symple synner thus space xx yeres perseuerynge holy lyfe reuelacyon lorde sholde retourne rome sholde accomplysshe terme lyfe martyrdome tolde kynge whi che ryght full sorowe answered sayd ala yf thou parte frome myne enemyes wyll assayle shall lose good fortune shall haue sayd hym thou kynge come leue thyne erthely royalme thou arte chosen posse noble kyngdome whiche without ende anone lefte wente holy vyrgyne lorde seruaūte come rome knowne crysten woman taken brought martyrdome whiche thynge kynge aeeya ryght sorowful ranne aboute wolde haue reuenged power yf holy vyrgyne bydden hym contrary soo wepte tenderly cryed cursed people moche euyll holy vyrgyne god came one sholde smyte heede yt blessyd vyrgyne ye kynge wente put heed cryenge crysten man offre myne heed ihesu cryst god maker thynge holy luce worshyppeth soo bothe heeded togyder crowned glory xij theym conuerted holy vyrgyne saynt luce wherof feest halowed togyder vij kalenders iule ¶ ye blessyd vyrgyne saynt martyne ca vj blessyd vyrgyne martyne maye forgoten blessyd mayde borne rome ryght noble kynred emperoure wolde constrayne wyfe bycau se beaute answered crysten woman offred god alyue whiche delyteth hym chaste bodyes clene herte hym sacrefyse commende despyte wordes emperoure made ledde temple constrayne worshyp ydolles veray seruaunt god tyraunte emperoure reuenge goddes made cruelly tourmented whiche god appered comforted prayed yt tourmented somoche conuerted merytes grete foyson people also ye whiche thynge emperoure worse dysposed made tourmented dyuers tourmentynges cruel tourmented thought verely yt sawe god sayntes asked mercy conuerted soo oryson prayenge lyght came rounde aboute voyce herde heuen sayd spare loue ryght welbyloued martyne prouost cryed conuerted sayd fooles ye deceyued en chauntresse martyne answered without drede nay thou arte deceyued dyuyll yt dwelleth within thou knowest hym made emperour wrothe measure cōmaunded hanged theyr flesshe al torne receyuynge martyr dome ioyfully praysed god emperour agayne made martyne dispoyled al naked flesshe whyte lylye yt made abasshed grete beaute emperour whiche coueyted longe tyme counsayled sawe wolde obaye made cutte al aboute woundes came mylke blode yelded grete swetnesse yet woode made stretche abrode raced hokes brake bo dy moche tourmented al wery god kepte sholde dye soone entente tourmentoures myght haue cause conuerted whiche began crye emperoure wyll aungelles beteth v chaynes came newe tormentoures tourment anone deed emperour cō fused wyste doo made stretched brenne brennynge gr • e alwaye gloryfyed lorde came mouthe ryght grete swetnesse tyrauntes tourmented moche ashamed cast derke pryson emenyon cosyn emperoure wen te loke pryson sawe martyne enuyronned aungelles set trone ryght well arayed grete clerenesse many dyuers songes ryght melodyous helde table golde y• whiche wry ten lorde swete ihesu cryst moche thy werkes praysed thy blessyd sayntes emenyon gretely admeruayled thynge wente tell emperoure whiche answered yt deceyued enchaūtementes ye mornynge tyraunt made taken pryson euery body meruaylled yt hole thrughe whiche many conuerted last made ledde tymple constrayne sacrefyse false goddes y• deuyll began braye sayd ala ala confounded holy vyrgyne commaunded hym come sholde shewe hym owne lewde lykenesse anone came grete thondre lyghtnynge came heuen brake ydoll brente ye preestes emperoure woode made stretched abrode raced y• flesshe body combes yron alway worshypped god sawe dyed made put wylde beestes deuoured grete lyon eten thre dayes came bowed hym laye downe lytell dog lycked woundes thanked lorde saynge blessyd thou almyghty god thy vertue hast modered cruelte wycked bestes tyraunte wrothe thynge commaunded lyon sholde put agayne caue ye lyon dressed hym grete wrathe made lepe slewe emenyon emperoures cosyn whiche thynge ryght sorowfull commaunded cast fyre beynge within ioyful chere god sente grete wynde put away fyre aboute brente tourmēted emperoure commaunded heere heed sholde cutte awaye • whiche ryght fayre longe sayenge enchauntementes heeres vyrgyne sayd hym thou takest awaye heeres whiche ornamente woman apostle sayth god shall put thy reygne poursue y• thou shalte byde dethe grete sorowe payne made enclosed temple goddes nayled dore sealed owne sygnete whē thre dayes past came agayne founde goddes ouerthrowne holy vyrgyne playenge aungelles hole sounde emperoure asked done wt goddes sayd y• vertue ihesu cryste hathe ouerthrowne blessyd martyne came bysshoppe rome clargye buryed y• body honourably y• chyrche ye day y• emperoure alexā der smyten suche sorowe yt ete owne flesshe gnewe hymselfe dethe ¶ saynt luce syracuse ca vij another vyrgyne saynt luce cyte syracuse prayed y• sepulture saynt agace moder whiche sy ke sawe saynt agace vysyon myddes aungelles arayed precyous stone whiche sayd luce syster deuoute vyrgyne wherfore requyrest thou yt thou mayst gyue thy moder thyselfe tell cer tayne y• y• cyte cathonyas lyfted vp shall cyte syracuse worshypped y• thou hast arayed ihesu cryst delectable iewelles thy clennesse luce rose vp moder hole gaue al goddes sake ended lyfe martyrdome amonge martyrdomes y• iuge manaced make ledde y• place yt lewde woman vsed theyr lyfe sholde defouled despyte spouse ydolles emperoure maxymy made sawed sawe yron • awyers seased sawynge fro houre tyerce anone houre noone myght entame sayd vertue hast thou holden v thyne en chauntementes soo longe without doynge ony thynge holy vyrgyne fauste began preche ihesu cryst lawe conuerted emperoure gre te indyngnacyon hereof made tour mented dyuers tourmentes amonge others made nayle heed thousan de nayles lyke helme without lepte cawdron twayne conuerted sawe y• lepte cawdron also whiche water boyled ryght feruently holy fauste touched theym▪and felte maner euyll sayd myddes byne beryn ge fruyte lorde sayth ben yonge souerayne beaute ouercame deuyll whiche called vp y• callynge • gromancere sholde mo che sholde consente wyll man gretely taken loue lefte pea prayer promyses coude doo nothynge trowed • eu • cypryen ben man ryght shrewde lyfe put good lyfe dyuers others conuerted y• sygnes yt god shewed ¶ also y• blessyd vyrgyne eulalye borne spay ne age xij yeres stale awaye fa der moder helde close desyrous go god prayed hym wolde take hym ended without touchynge ony wylde beestes ¶ vyrgyne theodosyne saynt barbara saynt dorothe ca ix constaunce martyrdome blessyd theodosyne cometh purpose well remēbred vyrgyne ryght noble grete beaute ye age xviij yeres meruayllous wytte dysputed iuge whiche manaced tourment yi forsoke ihesu cryst answered godly wordes made taken ye heere beten ryght sore sayd hym cer te caytyfe wolde lordeshyp another gouerne hymselfe ala hym hath grete charge fulfylled mete drynkes hath thought hongre euyl hym wolde warmed wyll clo ne warme ben euyll clothed wo hym wolde haue rest trauaylleth others euyll hym saythe thynges ben hathe receyued god wo hym wolde one sholde well dothe euyll suche worthy wordes sayd alwaye y• holy vyrgyne tourmente ¶ sorowe herte shame shamfast membres appered openly god sente whyte cloude couered al urban iuge manaced whome sayd thou west none meeses dyner ordeyned tyraunt manaced wolde corrupte vyrgynyte answered thou mana cest vayne corrupcyon god enha byteth ye clene hertes prouost wode made cast see heuy stone aboute necke borne vp aungelles brought agayne loude syngyn ge bare stone bytwene handes whiche wayed moche herselfe tyraunte made lette go vpon ij leoperdes lepte aboute makynge grete chere last tyraunt yt knewe howe made smyte heed soule departed fro body vysybly ye shappe whyte downe shynyn ge bryght nyght appered fa der moder clerer sone crowned precyous stoues accompanyed many vyrgynes holdynge crosse golde hande sayd se ioy ye wolde haue put awaye yt conuerted ¶ also ye tyme maxymyan emperoure floured vertues ye blessyd vyrgyne saynt barbara noble lygnage soueray nely sayre fader bycause beaute shytte toure inspyracyon ye crysten faythe yt myght baptysed none herselfe toke water baptysed name fader sone holy ghost fader wolde haue maryed ryght hyghly refused maryages laste tolde crystened hadde vowed vyrgynyte vnto god fader wolde haue slayne cause fledde escaped fader poursued put dethe laste founde ye techyn ge shepeherde whiche serched anone bothe hym beestes fader ledde y• prouost whiche dysobeyed al commaundementes made martyred many greuous tourmente hanged feete sayd hym caytyfe ne seest thou tourmentes dothe harme ryght wrothe made pappes drawne frome body estate made ledde thrughe cyte alwaye gloryfyed god hadde shame vyrgynall body sene naked lorde sente aungell heled woundes couered body whyte clothe ben ledde forth ynou ghe one ledde agayne prouost whiche wode sawe hole face shynynge bryght soo made agayne tourmented soo moche commaunded coude thynke mo tourmentes heed sholde smyten made orysons prayed god myght helpe requyred remembraū ce recorded passyon hadde ended oryson prayer voy ce herde heuen whiche sayd vnto wyse come vnto ryght dere welbyloued doughter rest kyngdome fader receyue thy crowne thou hast requyred shall graunted gone vp vpon y• hylle sholde heeded cruell fader smote heed hymselfe came downe hylle y• fyre heuen brent hym al poudre ¶ also y• blessyd vyrgyne saynt dorothe wyse suffred dyuers martyrdo me capadoce y• wolde take mā housbande spake moche spouse ihesu cryst mayster scoles whiche named theophylus sayd mockery one ledde heeded leest sholde spouse wolde sende hym rose apple gardyne housbande sayd wolde wherof happened soone made ende martyrdome ryght fayre yonge chylde y• age iiij yeres come theophylus brought hym lytell panyer full • ueraynly fayre rose apple meruayllously well smellynge fayre sayd yt vyrgyne dorothe sente hym gretely admeruaylled wryten moneth february conuerted martyred name ihesu cryst ¶ sayntes vyrgynes ben heuen constaunce martyrdome yf wolde tell y• hystory sholde ryght longe saynt cecyle saynt agnes saynt agace infynyte others yf thou wylte haue mo go behol de hystoryal myroure thou shalte fynde ynoughe shall tell yet saynt crystyne thy godmoder vyrgyne grete dygnyte shall tell lyfe playne whiche deuoute fayre ¶ lyfe saynt xp̄ine vyrgyne martyre capitulo x blessid vyrgyne saynt xp̄ine cyte syre doughter urban mayster cheualrye la dy beaute kepte close y• commaundement fader toure seuen maydens fader lete make fayre oratory ydolles nyghe chambre xp̄yne entente sholde worshyp yonge age xij yeres enspyred fayth ihesu cryst made ce ydolles wherof y• maydens meruaylled often tymes called oblacyon taken ensence make sacrefyse ydolles kneled towarde y• eest wyndowe loked towarde heuen encensed inmortall god moost parte nyght wyndowe beholdyn ge sterres waylynge besought god ry ght deuoutely prayed hym wolde helpe agaynst aduersaryes maydens whiche perceyued well herte ihesu cryste kneled often tymes ioyned handes prayenge yt sholde put entente straunge god yt wolde worshyp goddes fader moder yf knowne al sholde destroy ed saynt xp̄ine answered decey ued deuyll whiche styred worshyp many goddes one last fader knewe yt doughter wolde worshyp ydolles ryght sorowfull reproued sayd good wyll wolde offre god heuen trowed mente iupyter ryght glad wolde haue kyssed c • yed sayd foule mouthe wyll offre myne offrynge clene god heuen erthe yt fa der contente wente cham bre shytte fast dore set knee offred holy oryson god wepynge y• holy aungell lorde came downe comforted brought whyte brede mete wherof ete iij dayes maner mete drynke saynt xp̄ine sawe y• wyn dowes many poore crysten men beggynge fote toure hadde nothynge gyue wente seke idolles fader whiche golde syluer bra ke gaue peces poore men fader knewe thynge bete ryght cruelly tolde hym playnly deceyued worshyp suche false ymages one god trynyte whiche confessed god wolde worshyp dye therfore wherfore woode made bounde chaynes ledde betynge dyuers place put pryson sayd yt wolde iuge hymselfe cause soo made brought hym morowe manaced tourmentes yf wolde worshyp ydolles sa well wolde tourne entente prayer ne manaces made stryped naked bothe armes legges beten moche xij men wery asked fader alwaye yf aduysed sayd doughter naturall pyte constrayneth sore courage tourmente whiche arte flesshe reuerence faythe haue goddes constrayneth y• thou dyspysest theym holy vyrgyue answered hym tyraunt whiche ought calle fader enemye myne holynesse tourmente flesshe hardely thou haste engendred spare thou mayst wel doo thy pleasure spyryte whiche made fader whiche heuen thou hast power wyse touche temptacyon ihesu cryst sauyoure ke peth hym cruell fader woode made brynge whele let make made holy swete yonge mayden bounde put fyre vnder made cast boylynge oyle grete plentye vpō body whele tourned vpon brake god souerayne fader pyte seruaunt sente aungell whiche brake y• whele peces slewe tourmentoures staunched fyre delyuered vyrgyne ho le sounde slewe thousande persones behelde without pyte aungelles god came aboute comforted fader asked tell hath taught cursednesse answered tyraunt without pyte haue tolde well fader ihesu cryste hathe taught pacyence ryght way fayth god alyue therfore despyse thy tourmentes shall ouercome y• vertue god assaultes deuyll ouercome confused made cast ryght horryble derke pryson thynkyn ge grete mysteryes lorde came iij aungelles grete lyght brought mete comforted yelded thankynges god urban wyst lefte thynke tourmentes myght last anoy ed delyuered made put grete stone aboute necke throwe see anone threwe see aungelles receyued wente vp water aungelles xp̄ine prayed lorde ihesu cryst lyftynge vp eyen heuen myght please hym yt myght ceyue ye holy sacrament baptyme yt water whiche desyred moche haue lorde ihesu cryst dessended propre per sone grete multytude aungelles bap tysed made name xp̄ine crowned shynynge sterre vpon heed sette londe nyght urban tourmented y• deuyll dyed myscheuously y• mornynge founde prayenge faders halle corner thus blessyd xp̄ine whiche god wolde receyue matyrdome whiche desyred ryght moche ledde agayne tourmentoures pryson ¶ y• newe iuge named zyon whiche knewe well done made come hym coueyted beaute sawe fayre wordes aduayled hym made tourmented agayne made • ylle grete cawdron full oyle pytche grete fyre vndernethe foure men tourmented cawdron grete hokes yron holy vyrgyne songe god ryght melodyously mocked tourmentoures manaced paynes helle cruell iuge sawe yt nothynge aduayled hym made hange place people heere heed whiche longe shynynge lyke golde wo men came rennynge aboute whiche wepte pyte se yonge mayden tourmented cryed tyraunt sayenge thou vntrewe cruel man howe myght herte man haue suche cruelte agaynst mayden fayre tendre thou arte worse ony wylde beest wolde haue ronne vpon hym iuge sayd xp̄ine frende thou shalte suffre tourmente come let v worshyp y• souerayne god hath susteyned moche thought iupyter whiche helde theyr souerayne god thought otherwyse sayd hym thou hast ryght well sayd graunt made vn hanged ledde temple grete foy son people folowed whē brought ydolles trowynge wolde haue worshypped kneled downe behol dynge towarde heuen made oryson god rose vp tourned towarde ye ydoll sayd saye thou wycked spyryte whiche arte ydoll y• name ihesu cryst yt thou come anone y• wycked spyryte lepte made grete ferefull noyse y• whiche ferde fell downe erthe iuge releued sayd xp̄ine thou haste moued god almyghty hath pyte y• come myght se creature wrothe yt worde reproued hym strongly soo blynde knewe goddes vertue prayed god ydoll sholde falledowne al poudre y• whiche thynge done wor de sygnes ye holy mayde conuerted men woman mo iij thousande iuge ryght sore aferde sayd y• kynge knewe done agaynst god shewynge xp̄ine wolde destroye myscheuously iuge full angu y • waxed woode dyed ¶ thyrde iu ge came named iulyan made take xp̄ine made auaunt wolde make worshyp ydolles al myght coude myght make remeue place lete make grete fyre aboute bode yt fyre iij dayes iij nyghtes herde many dyuers swete melodyes tourmentoures aferde y• meruayllous sygnes yt sawe whiche thynges reported iulyan wende haue waxen wode whē y• fyre cōsumed came al hole iuge made serpentes brought forth made cast vpō ii aspes ij grete colubres whiche bote venymed meruayllously serpentes fell downe fete ye hedes enclyned towarde without doynge ony herme ij horrybie serpentes let lowce vpon hanged pappes lycked xp̄ine loked towarde heuen sayd yelde thankynges lorde god ihesu cryst whiche hast de worshypfully enhaunced holy vertues horryble serpentes knoweth thy dygnyte obstynate iulyan se ynge meruaylles cryed hym ke per serpentes arte thou enchaunted xp̄ine also whiche thou haste power moue serpentes agaynst whiche doubted iuge trowed haue moued serpentes ayenst ranne vpon hym slewe hym moche euery body doubted ye serpentes none durste come nyghe xp̄ine commaunded vertue god sholde go agayne theyr owne place wt doynge ony harme ony creature dyde raysed agayne ye deed man lyfe whiche anone cast hym feete conuerted iuge blynded ye deuyll perceyued meruayllous sygnes sayd vnto xp̄ine thou hast ynoughe shewed thy wytche craftes sayd hym thou man wytte yf thyne eyen wolde se y• vertues god thou sholdest byleue beyn ge passynge wrothe made drawe pappes body anone came mylke stede blode yt wtout seasynge named name lorde ihesus made cutte tonge spake better clerer dyde blessyd god thā kynge hym grete benefeytes dyde began make oryson vnto god yt myght please hym perfourme crowne martyrdome receyue hym herde voyce frome heuen sayen ge xp̄ine pure clene heuens ben open reygne without ende redy company sayntes blesseth god thou hast fro thy youthe susteyned name cryste praysed gloryfyed god eyen warde heuen voyce herde agayne whiche sayd come xp̄ine ryght welbyloued cho sen doughter receyue palme perdurable crowne ye rewarde thy passyonable lyfe confessyon name ye false iu lyan herde voyce blamed tourmentoures cutte tonge xp̄ine nerer cutte nyghe shol de speke moche dyde lorde ie su cryst toke yron hoke pulled tonge cutte anone ye throte toke culpen tonge threwe vysage tyraunt smote eye sayd hym holely euer spake thou cursed tyraunt auayleth cutte tonge ye entente yt sholde worshyp god spyryte shal alway worshyp hym thy spyryte shall dwell alway cursednesse yt thou knowest worde good reason yt tonge hathe made blynde whiche yt sawe ihesu cryste syttynge ryght syde fader ended martyrdome two arowes shotte one syde yt towarde ye herte cosyne whiche conuerted buryed body wro te gloryous legende blessyd xp̄ine holy mayden chosen god praye holynesse wherof god hath made soo worthy praye synner named thy name haue pyte blessyd godmoder whiche haste reioyced haue cause put thyne holy legende wrytynges whiche reuerence harecorded longe myght agreable woman cause good ensample ¶ dyuers sayntes whiche y• sawe theyr chyldren martyred ca xj thynge y• worlde ten dre moderly herte se chylde suffre payne yt se faythe yet grettest thynge appered many worshypfull woman whiche loue ihesu cryste offred theyr owne chyldren tourment blessyd felyx whiche sawe viij chyldren whiche ryght fayre yonglynges martyred comforted counsayled pacyence moderly wordes stable faythe loue god forgoten womanly courage body offred sacrefyse god wolde sacrefyed herselfe vnto god martyrdome ¶ also blessyd iulytte wyse whiche sonne named cyrycus nourysshed hym onely bodely fode also spy rytuall without seasynge enfourmed hȳ faythe suche wyse beynge ryght lytell yonge myght neuer ouercome tourmente ne fayre wordes sholde sake name ihesu cryste doughter whiche ye age xv yeres comforted ioyously woman sholde go spouse wente put tourmente soo moche tourmented multytude martyrdomes tourmen toures wery put agrydyren rosted alwaye prycked pynnes yron alwaye gloryfyed lorde god cōtynued anone y• dethe ¶ sholde saye fulfyll cyte suche meyny come saynt ursula thy xj thousande vyrgynes blessyd martyres y• name ihesu cryst theyr heedes smyten myght forgete abbot bad hȳ yt sholde go fetche y• myght put relygyon hym mayde fader clothed lytell monke coude well kepe close ryght good dyscyplyne came age xviij yeres alwaye perseuerynge frome good better y• fader whiche taught holy lyfe passed worlde abode alone faders celle holy lyuynge abbot praysed holy conuersacyon wyst none y• man abbay iij myles frome market towne fortuned monkes
