whiche named frere maryne dyuers tymes abo de course foresayd towne certayne hostery lodged communely came towne happe tyme doughter y• hoste chylde constrayned fader moder tell who put vpon frer • maryne wher fader moder came complayned abbot whiche made hym sente ryght sorowfull thynge holy may den leuer take blame vpon ex cuse kneled wepynge • ayd fader pray haue synned shall penaun ce abbot couent mōkes yt nyghe hym doughter waxen mo che ye fader wolde haue maryed yt gyuen purpose kepe vyrgynyte fled clothed ye guyse man requyred y• abbot yt myght receyued y• sayd abbaye made hym byleue abbot made fader brought doughter whiche knewe doughter knewe well y• fader anone full teeres tourned parte thoughe wolde ende maner oryson beaute fresshnesse vysage gretely empayred y• grete abstynence yt dyde spake fader comforted hym made hym certayne sholde se doughter dyed sholde doubte seruyce god euer yet sholde haue grete ioy fader trowed knewe dyuyne vertue departed then ryght well comforted sayd abbot euer syth doughter departed founde courage mo comforte sayd fulfylled grace god syth shall haue tydynges doughter recommendynge hym abbot prayer y• bretherne departed myght holde hym yt must often tymes come agayne vysyte ye ho ly brother dyde nothynge coun sayle thus endured longe tyme doughter whiche named herselfe synaroch complete space xxxviij yere within celle anastase vysyted sparynge nyght day prayed god wolde suffre lyue whyle goodes endured entente myght employ al holy werke emperoure commaunded dulcycyon prouost y• crysten peo ple y• prysons sholde accorde hym sholde delyuer theym refusynge put warde one y• famylyer hym made ledde house thought haue agaynst theyr wyll wt theyr wyll nyght came wente alone without lyght house made brought wolde goo place herde theyr voyce whiche nyght dyde thynge prayse god passed place vesselles kechyne kepte full deuyll blynded spyryte lechery god wolde toke necke kyssed straytely syth one syth another trowed yt ben maydens moche wente thus doyn ge y• verely wery daye wente people whiche abode hym wtout whiche sawe hym semed fygure deuyll moche soylled fatte cole gowne rente traylynge dyrte fledde hym aferde sawe fle thus despy sed hym meruayllously aba • ed wherfore thought hym wolde go complayne emperoure y• euery man mocked hym wente scorned hym entred y• palas whe many abode hym mornynge began grete crye vpon hym bete bȳ roddes shoued hym abacke sayenge go waye thou vnhappy abhomynable persone thou stynkest aboute scrat ched hym y• vysage laughed hym scorne soo greately admeruaylled myght almoost wytte deuyll closed soo eyen myght perceyue tourned hym home agayne vnto house ryght foule ashamed ¶ another iuge put place whiche made thre blessyd vyrgynes come hym wolde make worshyppe ydolles wolde nothynge byddynge commaū ded dyspoyled naked soo beten yet theyr myght myght despoyle theym theyr clothes cleuynge myght man put made put fyre ryght hote brennynge whiche greued nothynge prayed god myght ende theyr ly ues yf pleased hym passed anone lorde ryght gloryously showe theyr wyll dye fyre neuer brente none theyr clothes fyre wasted bodyes founde han de ioyned hole fresshe thoughe slepte blessyd lady anastase whiche toke good hede buryed ¶ saynt theodore vyrgyne ca xv another noble felawe good anastase whiche named theo dory whiche iij yonge chyldren lady refused maryage erle lencadyne yt wolde sacrefyse ydolles made many tourmentes constrayne better moderly pyte made tourment one sone vertue ye faythe whiche passed nature comforted hym sayenge sone ne martyres tourmented confessed name ihesu cryst wherfore ye em perour ryght wrothe made hym put ryght harde pryson good lady ryght ioyous ye conuersyon housbande wente anone ye pryson comforte hym praye hym perseuer begon kyssed chaynes whiche bounde wepyn ge pyte ioye counsayllynge hym grete ly wolde haue respecte erthely ioyes endured whyle shol de haue eyen grete glory ordeyned hym holy lady lon ge comfortynge hym martyres praynge god myght theyr company prayed gretely sholde comfor te housbande whome doubted force tourmentes sholde chaunge stablenesse faythe vysyted hym eue ry daye euery daye preched hym haue stablenesse many fayre worde spake hym dyuers ladyes vy syted holy martyres emperoure made defende woman sholde come therfore clothed guyse man came daye last martyrdome presente wyped woundes kyssed blode prayed hym wol de pray god thus passed blessyd adryan toke one handes cutte wrapped full derely couerchefe relyke holy lady dethe housbande one wolde constrayne wedded bycause hyghe lygnage fayre ryche alway oryson pray enge god wolde drawe han de wolde constrayne wedded appered slepynge ye spyryte housbande whiche comforted sayd vnto sholde goo coustantynoble burye bodyes many martyres dyde soo ben whyle goddes seruyce vy sytynge holy martyres emprysoned housbande appered vnto agayne sayd syster frende chambere ihesu cryste co glorye perpetuall lorde calleth awoke anone passed lorde ¶ holy blessyd saynt affra capitulo xvij affra woman lyued folyly conuerted fayth ihesu cryst accused iuge whiche sayd suffyseth ye dyshonestye thy body yt thou muste fall erroure worshyp straunge god sacrefyse goddes maye pardon affra answered shall doo sacrefyse god ihesu cryste came downe synners gospell sayth yt woman synner wassh ed feete teres forgyuenesse despysed neuer folyly lyuynge womā ne ye publycanes synners lete ete wt hym iuge sayd vnto thou sacrefyse thou shalte loued thy rybaudes ne thon shalte receyue gyftes answered shal neuer receyue cursed gyftes yt haue goten vntruely haue prayed poore peo ple wyll take pray fyn ne iuge gaue sētence saynt affra sholde brente syth wolde sacrefyse delyuered tourmente worshypped god sayd lorde god almyghty ihesu cryst whiche callest synners penaunce receyue martyrdome goood entente houre passyon delyuer fro euerlastynge fyre corporall fyre arayed body ye fyre beynge aboute sayd lorde ihesu cryst pleaseth ye receyue pore synner sacrefyse thy holy name y• y• offred thyselfe sacrefyse worlde thou ryghtfull put crosse vnryghtfull good euyll doer blessyd cursed swete bytter clene innocent synne delyuer synners offre sacrefyse body whiche lyueth reygneth fader holy ghost worlde worldes thus ended blessyd affre whome lorde hath shewed syth many myracles ¶ telleth iustyce dyuers ladyed whiche serued lodged appostles sayntes capitulo xviii woldest thou saye fayre xp̄ine myght brynge remembraunce suche ensamples without nombre y• thou arte adme ruaylled thou haste sayd wherfore auctours blame woman saye thoughe thou hast founde wrytynges auctours pay nymes trowe purpose thou sha • te fynde fewe holy legendes hysto rye ihesu cryst appostles wyse sayntes thou mayst se grete nombre thou shalte fynde meruayl lous constauncè grace god woman good seruyces grete charytees haue ne without faynynge good wyll y• seruaūtes god bothe hospytalytees good dedes wryten drucyane whiche good lady awydowe whiche ceyued host saynt iohn̄ euangelyst serued hym mete drynke whan sayd saynt iohan sholde receyued fro exyle cyte made hym grete feest drucyane borne buryed whiche deed sorowe yt taryed longe neygh boures sayd hym iohan see drucyane thy good hostesse whiche deed sorowe thy longe taryenge shal serue y• saynt iohan sayd drucyane ryse vp go thy house make redy refeccy rose frome dethe lyfe ¶ also another ye cyte lymoges named susanne fyrst harboured saynt marcyall whiche sente thyder saynt peter conuerte countre dyde hym ryght moche good ¶ also good lady maxymylle buryed saynt androwe toke hym frome crosse doynge put herselfe peryll dethe ¶ also ye holy mayde euphygene folowed denocyon saynt mathewe euangelyst dethe made edefye hym ryght fayre chyrche ¶ also another good lady moche taken wt loue saynt poule ye apostle folowed hym aboute serued hym grete dylygence ¶ also yt tyme ye apostle noble quene called helyn y• moder constantyne another quene oblygoys whiche wente iherusalem whiche grete scarcete vytaylles famyne knewe sayntes lorde ye cyte preche conuerte people dyed hongre made bye moche vytaylles pouruayed longe derthe lasted ¶ also one lydde saynt poule heeded commaundement nero good lady whiche called pautylle acostomed serue hym came ayenst hym wepynge gretely saynt poule asked couerchefe vpon heed toke hym wherof shrewde people yt mocked hym sayenge fayre moche loste saynt poule hymselfe wyped eyen deed sente agayne woman full blode wherfore kepte ryght rychely saynt poule appered sayd moche done hym seruyce heuen prayenge ynoughe others lyke case myght tell ¶ uaxyllete noble lady vertue charyte lady maryed saynt iulyan nyght theyr weddynge one acorde vowed vyrgynyte none myght thynke holy conuersacyon woman ne y• multytude woman maydens saued drawne holy lyfe holy monycyon saye shortely moche grace lorde spake dyenge ¶ wote sholde saye xp̄yne dere loue myght tell without nombre ladyes dyuers estate well vyrgynes wydowes maryed woman whome god hath shewed vertues meruayllous strengthe constaun ce thou suffysed nowe ryght well fayre semeth haue wel quytte ne offyce perfourmynge hyghe bataylementes thy cyte haue peopled excellente ladyes promysed notwithstandynge name ne maye name holy ladyes theyr name whiche yt hathe ben whiche ben whiche shal maye comprehended cyte ladyes whiche one maye saye ¶ gloriosa dictum sunt de te ciuitas dei say gloryous thynges ben sayd thou cyte god yelde parfyte thynge wel stably promysed nowe betake god pea oure hyghe souerayne euerlastyngely amen ¶ xp̄ine speketh vnto ladyes ende boke ca xix mi ryght redoubted ladyes worshyp ped god nowe cyte well accheued made parfyte whiche ye loueth honoure vertue praysynge may lodged grete worshyp wel past ben nowe come founded made euery woman worshyp ryght dere ladyes thynge natural mannes herte reioyce hym fyndeth hym hathe vyctory ony entrepryse enemyes confounded haue ye cause ye ladyes reioyce nowe vertuously god good cōdycyons newe cyte se parfyte whiche may onely refuge al vnderstan de vertuous woman also defence warde ayenst enemyes assayllers yf ye kepe well ye may se matter wherof made vertue truely shynynge ye maye beholde therin specyally y• emfrytaylynge laste partye wyse whiche may touche par tyes dere ladyes soo vse ye newe herytage proude people whiche come full pryde whē theyr prosperyte encrea seth mounted rychesse y• ensample quene souerayne vyrgyne whiche grete worshyp aungell brought moder sone god moche meked callynge y• hande mayden god ladyes true vertues ben ye ought yel de humble benygne cyte cause vnto loue good maners vertuous humble ¶ haue ye despyte ye ladyes ben maryed subiectes housbandes tymes beste creature free subieccyon wytnesseth tonge lorde god sayth esoras prophete sayth vse theyr free wyll falleth synne despyse theyr lorde defouleth iuste people therfore perysshe ye humble pa • yente grace god shall encreace ye shal gyuen praysynge y• worlde saynt gregory sayth pacyence entrye paradyse way ihesu cryst ¶ amon vyrgynes state maydenhode ye clene symple coye without ydelnesse y• gynne euyll men ben set agaynst ye armed vertuous strengthe agaynst theyr cauteyles eschewe theyr frequentacyon ¶ ladyes wedowes honest habyte countenaunce worde deuoute dede conuersacyon prudente gouernaunce pacyente nede mekenesse charyte ¶ generally grete meane lytel wyll ye alway set defence agaynst ene myes worshyp chastyte se ladyes howe accuseth maketh lyers blameth put abacke losen gyers whiche dyuers draughtes hurteth withdraweth ye ought kepe well vnderstande worshyppes lewde loue whiche counsayle styreth therto fle goddes loue fle ye certayne thoughe semblaunt fayre deceyuable tymes ende preiudyce thynke contrary otherwyse maye remembre howe call frayle false alwaye seke en gynes ryght straunge deceyuable grete payne trauayle take one take wylde beestes flee theyr gynne ladyes flee theyr acquayntaunce vnder laughyn ge whome lapped venyme ryght full anguysshe whiche bryngeth one lyghtly dethe thus please ryght redoubted ladyes drawe vertues flee vyces encreace multeplye cyte ye reioy ce well doynge seruaunt commended vnto praynge god whiche grace worlde graunte lyue perseuer holy seruyce ende pyteous grete defautes graunte bothe vnto ioye whiche endureeuermore amen ¶ finis ¶ endeth thyrde last partye
